three rangers of the night's watch ser <WAYMAR> <ROYCE> , will , and <GARED> depart from the wall to investigate reports of <WILDLINGS> in the haunted <FOREST> which lies to the north , <BEYOND> the wall . will , the best scout in the group , discovers a number of wildling corpses dismembered and arranged in a strange , ritualistic fashion on the ground . 
wight of wildling girl . he also finds a dead wildling girl pinned to a tree . he reports back to the others . ser <WAYMAR> overrides the older <GARED>'s advice that they return to <CASTLE BLACK> to report the situation to their superiors and instead insists on seeing the corpses for himself , to determine what killed them . when they reach the site , the bodies have disappeared . will scouts around for clues , but <GARED> finds a bloody piece of clothing buried under the snow . further investigations are curtailed when a tall , humanoid figure with glowing blue eyes , a white walker , arrives and kills ser <WAYMAR> with ease . <GARED> attempts to escape but is caught and killed . will , in extreme horror , sees the dead wildling girl from earlier now walking with blue eyes , and also witnesses <GARED>'s death , with the white walker tossing his severed head at will's feet .

 <NED STARK> draws his sword . 
some time later , will has fled <SOUTH> of the wall in terror , rather than return to warn <CASTLE BLACK> of the white walker threat . he is apprehended by outriders loyal to <HOUSE STARK> , the wardens of the north , and is taken to lord <EDDARD STARK> . lord <EDDARD STARK> , in the courtyard watching his son , <BRAN STARK> at archery training , decrees that as a deserter from the watch , will is an <OATHBREAKER> and must die . will accepts his fate , but tells <EDDARD STARK> about the walkers first and asks that word be sent back to his mother . <EDDARD STARK> carries out the execution himself , using the ancestral <VALYRIAN> blade of their <HOUSE STARK> , <ICE> . two of <EDDARD STARK>'s trueborn sons , 17 year old robb and 10 year old <BRAN STARK> , accompany him to the execution along with his bastard son <JON SNOW> , his ward , <THEON GREYJOY> , the master at arms <RODRIK CASSEL> and his leading guard <JORY CASSEL> . young <BRAN STARK> witnesses an execution for the first time without flinching , earning praise from <JON SNOW> . <EDDARD STARK> explains to <BRAN STARK> that the reason he was made to execute will was because the man who passes the sentence should swing the sword . when <BRAN STARK> asks his father about will's talk of <WHITE WALKERS> , <EDDARD STARK> dismisses it as a madman's ramblings , insisting that the <WHITE WALKERS> have been gone for centuries . the party sets out to return to winterfell . 
the <STARKS> come across the direwolves . 
on the way back to the <CASTLE BLACK> , the party finds a stag dead in the road , partially disemboweled . looking for what killed it , they find a dead female direwolf , killed with a stag antler piece broken off in her throat . the female died after giving birth , and her five pups huddle by the corpse for warmth . <THEON GREYJOY> advocates killing the pups , but <JON SNOW> convinces his father that this is an omen the direwolf is the symbol of <HOUSE STARK> , and <EDDARD STARK> has five trueborn children . with <BRAN STARK> looking on beseechingly , <EDDARD STARK> agrees that his children should have the pups , but only if they raise them themselves with no help from the servants . just as the party leaves , <JON SNOW> finds a sixth pup , an albino runt of the litter . <THEON GREYJOY> mockingly points out that this one belongs to <JON SNOW> . 
in king's <LANDING> , the capital city of the <SEVEN KINGDOMS> , the bells ring out to commemorate the death of lord <JON ARRYN> , the <HAND> of the king . as the <SILENT SISTERS> prepare his body for burial , queen <CERSEI LANNISTER> looks on . she is worried that <JON ARRYN> discovered something he shouldn't have , and may have told someone . she confesses her fears to her twin brother , ser <JAIME LANNISTER> of the <KINGSGUARD> , but he tells her not to worry , since if the king knew the truth they'd be dead already . she tells him he should be the new <HAND> of the king , but he doesn't want the job . he considers it too much work . <CERSEI LANNISTER> accuses him of taking nothing seriously . 
a raven bears news of <JON ARRYN>'s death to winterfell , where lady <CATELYN STARK> informs <EDDARD STARK> . he is particularly stricken because <JON ARRYN> served as a father figure to him , when he was fostered at the <EYRIE> . she also tells him that king <ROBERT BARATHEON> and much of the royal court rides for winterfell . <EDDARD STARK> realizes that king <ROBERT BARATHEON> means to name him as the <HAND> to replace <JON ARRYN> . he ponders refusing , feeling his place is at winterfell . 
over the next few weeks the <EDDARD STARK> children grow used to their rapidly growing direwolves robb names his <GREY WIND> , sansa calls hers lady , and arya names hers <NYMERIA> after a great warrior queen . <JON ARRYN> names his ghost , for his <WHITE WALKERS> color and uncanny silence . <BRAN STARK> calls his <SUMMER> and six year old <RICKON> names his wolf <SHAGGYDOG> . <BRAN STARK>'s mother catches him climbing on the rooftops of the <CASTLE BLACK> , just as the royal party comes into view . he promises to stop , but his mother knows he is lying . winterfell prepares for guests . <CATELYN STARK> wants to make sure that <TYRION LANNISTER> , a great reader , has enough candles , and the young men of the <HOUSE STARK> get groomed , as they gossip about the queen , a reportedly great beauty . 
winterfell gathers to greet the royal party . 
all of winterfell gathers in the courtyard as the royal party approaches . arya is late and annoys sansa by not being <SILENT SISTERS> and respectful when they arrive . king <ROBERT BARATHEON> rides in with his knights , while queen <CERSEI LANNISTER> is in a large wheelhouse . lord <EDDARD STARK> presents his household to king <ROBERT BARATHEON> . <EDDARD STARK> and <ROBERT BARATHEON> greet each other warmly , and then <ROBERT BARATHEON> demands to see the crypts and pay his respects to <EDDARD STARK>'s deceased sister , lyanna , much to queen <CERSEI LANNISTER>'s impatience . after <ROBERT BARATHEON> and <EDDARD STARK> depart , <CERSEI LANNISTER> sends <JAIME LANNISTER> to find their younger brother <TYRION LANNISTER> , who is a dwarf . the <IMP> has found his way to the brothel in the <TOWN> <OUTSIDE> winterfell , where he enjoys the attentions of a prostitute named ros . <JAIME LANNISTER> tells <TYRION LANNISTER> , a man of limited height but with immense appetites , that he will be needed at the feast that night . <JAIME LANNISTER> has hired three more prostitutes for <TYRION LANNISTER> , to hurry things along . 
lyanna's statue in the crypts of winterfell . 
in the crypts <ROBERT BARATHEON> offers up his prayers at the tomb of <LYANNA STARK> , <EDDARD STARK>'s younger sister , whom <ROBERT BARATHEON> was betrothed to before she was kidnapped by prince <RHAEGAR TARGARYEN> and died shortly after being rescued . he tells <EDDARD STARK> that in his dreams he kills <RHAEGAR TARGARYEN> every night anew . <EDDARD STARK> reminds him that <HOUSE TARGARYEN> was destroyed , but <ROBERT BARATHEON> replies not all of them . 
 <ROBERT BARATHEON> formally offers <EDDARD STARK> the role of <HAND> , and <EDDARD STARK> asks for time to consider . <ROBERT BARATHEON> agrees , but offers a sweetener the <HAND> of his son , joffrey , in marriage to <EDDARD STARK>'s daughter , sansa . a great feast is held and <CERSEI LANNISTER> and <CATELYN STARK> exchange cordial words . <CERSEI LANNISTER> seems more impressed by sansa , thinking that she will be a great hit at court . <OUTSIDE> the feast , <JON SNOW> works at his sword practice , angry that <CATELYN STARK> thought it would be inappropriate that a bastard should attend . his uncle <BENJEN> <CATELYN STARK> , first ranger of the night's watch , arrives to join the feast , and <JON SNOW> asks him to take him back to the wall with him . <BENJEN> agrees to consider it . <TYRION LANNISTER> then arrives and talks to <JON SNOW> , suggesting that he is too pricklish and quick to take offense when his illegitimacy is pointed out . he should take the insult and wear it like armor , so that no one can hurt him with it . when <JON SNOW> angrily asks <TYRION LANNISTER> what he knows about it , <TYRION LANNISTER> replies that all dwarfs are bastards in their father's eyes . 
 <EDDARD STARK> and <CATELYN STARK> receive a letter in the night , delivered to maester <LUWIN> by a messenger from the <EYRIE> . the letter is from <CATELYN STARK>'s sister , lady <LYSA ARRYN> , the widow of <JON ARRYN> . in the letter , <LYSA ARRYN> says that <JON ARRYN> was murdered by the <LANNISTERS> and that they plan to conspire against king <ROBERT BARATHEON> . <LUWIN> counsels that <EDDARD STARK> should accept <ROBERT BARATHEON>'s offer to be <HAND> , so he can investigate the truth of the matter and protect the king . <EDDARD STARK> , while he would prefer to stay at winterfell , agrees with <LUWIN> and accepts the offer . 
the next morning <EDDARD STARK> and <ROBERT BARATHEON> go hunting , leaving the <CASTLE BLACK> largely empty . <BRAN STARK> indulges in some climbing but , while climbing a <BROKEN TOWER> , he hears someone moaning . he peers through a window and finds the queen and her brother engaged in a sexual act . <CERSEI LANNISTER> spots him and warns <JAIME LANNISTER> , who grabs <BRAN STARK> . <JAIME LANNISTER> looks out the window to make sure nobody else is watching and only sees <SUMMER> . he turns to <BRAN STARK> and asks how old he is . when <BRAN STARK> replies ten , <JAIME LANNISTER> remarks with a sigh , the things i do for love . with that , he pushes <BRAN STARK> out of the window .

in the free city of <PENTOS> , across the <NARROW SEA> , <VISERYS> and <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> enjoy the hospitality of magister <ILLYRIO> mopatis . <VISERYS> has arranged to wed his sister <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> also called <DANY> to <KHAL DROGO> , the warlord of a dothraki khalasar of forty thousand warriors . in return , <KHAL DROGO> will give <VISERYS> the <ARMY> he needs to reclaim the <IRON THRONE> . <VISERYS> prepares <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> for meeting the <KHAL DROGO> . he tells her what a beautiful young woman she has turned into , and slips off her dress and fondles her breast . she is <SILENT SISTERS> and looks away as if pretending it isn't happening . she steps into a hot bath that has just been poured . this greatly distresses her maid who believes the water will scald her . however , <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> seems not to notice it and appears to be unharmed . 
 <KHAL DROGO> arrives in <PENTOS> and approves of <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> . 
 <ILLYRIO> and <VISERYS> discuss the quest to sail back to westoros , and <VISERYS> inquirers when the wedding will take place . <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> is not pleased with the arrangement and blurts out that she does not want to marry <KHAL DROGO> . <VISERYS> insists that she will , because in return <KHAL DROGO> will give him the <ARMY> he needs to retake their father's <IRON THRONE> from <ROBERT BARATHEON> . <VISERYS> adds that he would let her be raped by all forty thousand of <KHAL DROGO>'s men and their horses if it meant getting his <IRON THRONE> back . a short time later , <KHAL DROGO> arrives at <ILLYRIO>'s estate . after taking a glance at <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> , <KHAL DROGO> rides away without having to dismount from his horse . <VISERYS> is concerned , but <ILLYRIO> assures him that , if he did not approve of <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> , they would have known . 
 <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> in her wedding dress . 
later , <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> marries <KHAL DROGO> and a great celebration is held . several people die in impromptu duels , which <ILLYRIO> says is a good sign a dothraki wedding without at least three deaths is considered a dull affair . the bride and groom receive many gifts , but for <DANY> , two are particularly interesting . the first is a box containing three beautiful stones . according to <ILLYRIO> , these are dragon eggs from the <SHADOW> lands <BEYOND> asshai that have turned to stone with the passing of time . <DANY> appears to feel some connection with the eggs , but brushes it off for the time being . the second is a selection of books containing stories and songs from the <SEVEN KINGDOMS> , given by ser <JORAH MORMONT> , an exiled knight of <HOUSE MORMONT> . ser <JORAH MORMONT> swears fealty to <VISERYS> as king and offers him his support and advice , which is accepted . for his gift , <KHAL DROGO> gives <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> a beautiful white stallion . <VISERYS> asks his sister to make <KHAL DROGO> happy . <KHAL DROGO> and <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> ride down to the shore and consummate their marriage on the beach at sunset . <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> is visibly upset and terrified . 
winter is coming is the first episode of the first season of game of thrones , preceded only by an unaired pilot episode . it first aired on 17 <APRIL> 2011. a 15 minute preview of the first episode was shown on 3 <APRIL> 2011. the episode was written by executive producers david benioff d.b . <WEISS> and directed by tim van patten . 
king <ROBERT BARATHEON> majestically arrives in winterfell , the <HOME> of his old and trusted friend , <EDDARD STARK> , warden of the north , with an important offer . 

the dothraki khalasar led by <KHAL DROGO> have departed <PENTOS> and are heading east . they travel away from the <FREE CITIES> and into the dothraki <NARROW SEA> , the long grassed plains that the dothraki call <HOME> . <VISERYS> <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> accompanies the khalasar , meaning to stay with <KHAL DROGO> until he fulfills his end of the bargain and provides him with an <ARMY> with which to invade <WESTEROS> , despite ser <JORAH MORMONT>'s suggestion . he tells <VISERYS> that he offended his liege lord , <EDDARD STARK> , by selling poachers into slavery . when he received word that <EDDARD STARK> meant to execute him for the crime slavery has been illegal in <WESTEROS> for centuries , he fled to essos . <VISERYS> laughs at the notion , saying such trivialities would not be punished under his reign . <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> is finding adapting to her new role as khaleesi to be a huge challenge . only <JORAH MORMONT> offers her some solace saying it will become easier . <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> is however fearful of her new husband and it is revealed that their first sexual encounter has left her slightly injured . 
fascinated with her gift from <ILLYRIO> , <DANY> asks her handmaidens if they have ever heard of dragons surviving in the east . they reply no , but <DOREAH> , a former pleasure girl from <LYS> , tells her an old story about how there used to be two moons in the sky . one wandered too close to the sun and cracked like an <EGG> , spilling out thousands of dragons into the world . <DANY>'s dothraki handmaidens <IRRI> and jhiqui dismiss the story , saying that the moon is a goddess , wife to the sun . 
 <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> seeks the advice of her handmaid <DOREAH> . <DOREAH> instructs <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> on how to please <KHAL DROGO> in bed but also how to use her skills to gain respect from him . reminding her , you are no slave and should not have sex like one . <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> nervously puts these plans into action and is surprised to find <KHAL DROGO> responsive , particularly once she starts using her body in combination with the dothraki language to speak to him .

in winterfell , <BRAN STARK> lies unconscious and badly wounded , his mother by his side . <TYRION LANNISTER> insists that his nephew joffrey pay his respects to lord and lady <BRAN STARK> , since his absence has been noted . when joffrey refuses , saying the boy means nothing to him , <TYRION LANNISTER> slaps him three times until he accepts his uncle's suggestion . <TYRION LANNISTER> then breakfasts with his other family members , informing them of his decision to journey north to see the wall before returning to king's <LANDING> . he also tells them that <BRAN STARK> is expected to live and notes cersei and <JAIME LANNISTER>'s guarded reactions . 
cersei visits <CATELYN STARK> , sitting by her son's side , and tells her that her first child , a beautiful , black haired boy , died of a fever . she and <ROBERT BARATHEON> were grief stricken and her prayers and tears were for naught . she offers to pray for <BRAN STARK>'s survival , hoping that this time the gods will listen . 
 <JON SNOW> has winterfell's blacksmith , mikken , forge a <LIGHT> sword for his sister , arya . arya is excited by the gift and names it <NEEDLE> . <JON SNOW> also gives her advice on how to best use the weapon stick them with the pointy end . <JON SNOW> urges arya to practice every chance she gets . <JON SNOW> then says goodbye to the comatose <BRAN STARK> , before departing at his stepmother's cold request . <EDDARD STARK> then says his goodbyes to his son and to <CATELYN STARK> , who is angered at his departure while <BRAN STARK> remains ill. . 
the two parties depart winterfell . 
the parties depart winterfell <JON SNOW> , <TYRION LANNISTER> and <BENJEN> <BRAN STARK> to the wall and <EDDARD STARK> , arya , sansa and the royal party <SOUTH> to king's <LANDING> . at their parting <EDDARD STARK> tells <JON SNOW> that , though he does not have <EDDARD STARK>'s name , he has his blood . he also promises <JON SNOW> to tell him about his mother the next time they meet . . 
 <EDDARD STARK> says goodbye to his bastard son . 
days later , on the <KINGSROAD> <SOUTH> to the capital , king <ROBERT BARATHEON> calls a halt to discuss with <EDDARD STARK> some dire news that has just arrived . <ROBERT BARATHEON>'s spies have learned of <DAENERYS TARGARYEN>'s marriage to <KHAL DROGO> , whose khalasar is reported to number over one hundred thousand warriors . <EDDARD STARK> points out that the dothraki can not cross the <NARROW SEA> , as they have no ships , but <ROBERT BARATHEON> is concerned that the <SEVEN KINGDOMS> will soon face another war . a curious <ROBERT BARATHEON> asks <EDDARD STARK> about wylla , the mother of his bastard son , but <EDDARD STARK> refuses to enlighten him . <ROBERT BARATHEON> reminds him that they were in the middle of a war and no one knew if they would ever return to their families . 
in winterfell , <CATELYN STARK>'s refusal to leave <BRAN STARK>'s side is starting to cause problems for the smooth running of the castle . <ROBB STARK> offers to work with maester <LUWIN> to put the castle to rights . there is then a fire in part of the castle , but this proves to be a distraction to allow an assassin to attempt to finish off <BRAN STARK> . <CATELYN STARK> holds the assassin off long enough for <BRAN STARK>'s direwolf to enter the chamber and tear out the assassin's throat . 
 <JON SNOW> and <TYRION LANNISTER> discussing matters . 
traveling north , <JON SNOW> and <TYRION LANNISTER> talk , and <TYRION LANNISTER> reveals that he reads books to sharpen his mind , his greatest asset and weapon . as it travels north , the party is joined by several , new recruits rapists who chose to take the black , rather than face the knife . <TYRION LANNISTER> tells <JON SNOW> that the night's watch is not a noble institution of glorious knights defending the <REALM> against the horrors lurking <BEYOND> the wall , but a dumping ground for the unwanted and for criminals . 
in winterfell , <CATELYN STARK> goes to the tower from where <BRAN STARK> fell and finds a strand of blonde hair on the floor . she summons <ROBB STARK> , <ROBERT BARATHEON> , <LUWIN> and the castle master at arms , ser <RODRIK CASSEL> and tells them that she suspects that the <LANNISTERS> tried to kill <BRAN STARK> because he might have seen something in the tower . <ROBB STARK> and <ROBERT BARATHEON> are all for making war , but <LUWIN> schools them to caution . <CATELYN STARK> decides that ned must know the truth and resolves to travel <SOUTH> to king's <LANDING> and meet him there . ser <RODRIK CASSEL> will go as escort , while <ROBB STARK> will take charge of the castle in her absence . . 
the wall , as seen by <JON SNOW>'s party . 
 <JON SNOW>'s party crests a rise and sees the wall before them . <BENJEN> welcomes them , and <TYRION LANNISTER> seems impressed by the wall's sheer size . 
on the <KINGSROAD> , the royal party reaches the <CROSSROADS INN> , a noted waystop on the way <SOUTH> to the capital . prince joffrey's bodyguard , <SANDOR CLEGANE> , known as the <HOUND> , a man with half his face burned in a mysterious accident , introduces sansa to ser <ILYN PAYNE> , the king's headsman , a frightening looking man who had his tongue torn out on the orders of the <MAD> king many years ago . joffrey saves sansa from this unpleasantness and takes her for a walk along the riverbank . they find arya practicing her sword work with the son of the party's butcher , <MYCAH> . joffrey pretends to take offense at <MYCAH> using a sword on the sister of his betrothed and starts to gleefully cut <MYCAH>'s face with his sword , but an outraged arya hits him on the head with a stick . joffrey quickly becomes violent and threatens arya at sword point , but before he can hurt her , arya's direwolf , <NYMERIA> , attacks joffrey , biting at his arm . <MYCAH> runs off , and arya throws joffrey's sword in the river before running off herself . sansa tries to help joffrey , but he spitefully tells her to leave him alone and go for help . 
arya , knowing that <NYMERIA> will be punished for injuring the prince , forces the direwolf to flee by throwing a rock at her . she is then taken before the king , who is angered that a minor fracas has become a major incident , with his wife and new <HAND> blaming one another's children . he decides to let ned discipline arya while he will do the same to joffrey , but cersei demands that the direwolf be executed . when <NYMERIA> can not be found , cersei spitefully requests that sansa's direwolf lady be killed instead , and <ROBERT BARATHEON> acquiesces , upsetting sansa and angering arya . 
furious , <EDDARD STARK> attends to the matter himself , passing the <HOUND> arriving with <MYCAH>'s bloodied corpse . <EDDARD STARK> is shocked and disgusted , and when he asks if the <HOUND> ran <MYCAH> down , the <HOUND> responds he ran , but not very fast . <EDDARD STARK> kills lady with a dagger , and hundreds of miles away , <BRAN STARK> awakens . 
the <KINGSROAD> is the second episode of the first season of game of thrones . it is the second episode of the series overall . it first aired on <APRIL> 24 , 2011. it was written by executive producers david benioff d.b . <WEISS> and directed by tim van patten . 
 <JON SNOW> prepares to depart for the wall . 

the <BRAN STARK> party arrives in king's <LANDING> . 
the royal party reaches king's <LANDING> . almost immediately , lord <EDDARD STARK> is asked to attend a meeting of the king's <SMALL COUNCIL> and to change his clothes , but he refuses to the latter . before that he encounters <JAIME LANNISTER> in the throne room . <JAIME LANNISTER> is still unhappy that <EDDARD STARK> judged him dishonorable for killing the <MAD> king , the murderer of <EDDARD STARK>'s father and brother . <JAIME LANNISTER> is unrepentant about it . <EDDARD STARK> meets the <SMALL COUNCIL> members lord <PETYR> <LITTLEFINGER> baelish , the king's master of coin and a friend of <EDDARD STARK>'s wife from childhood <GRAND> maester <PYCELLE> , the king's adviser in all matters scientific and academic lord <RENLY> <ROBERT BARATHEON> , the youngest of the king's two <BROTHERS> and master of laws and <VARYS> , a eunuch and the master of whisperers the head of the king's intelligence network . 
 <VARYS> tells <EDDARD STARK> that the <SMALL COUNCIL> members heard about his troubles on the <KINGSROAD> and that they pray for joffrey's recovery . <EDDARD STARK> grimly responds it's a shame no one prayed for the butcher's boy , which visibly upsets <VARYS> . 
 <EDDARD STARK> is stunned to learn that the crown is six million gold dragons in debt , half of which is to lord <TYWIN LANNISTER> . to make matters worse , king <ROBERT BARATHEON> has just ordered a lavish tournament to celebrate <EDDARD STARK>'s appointment . he resolves to advise <ROBERT BARATHEON> to cancel the tournament , but the <SMALL COUNCIL> is doubtful that the king will listen . 
cersei and her son joffrey . 
queen cersei talks to joffrey about the incident on the river . she tells him that when he is king , the truth will be whatever he decides it will be . joffrey thinks there will be trouble with the <STARKS> , and promises that when he is king , he will double their taxes , force them to contribute to a standing <ARMY> and , should they object , crush them and install someone loyal , such as his great uncle <KEVAN> , as warden of the north . cersei points out that the north is too vast and wild to be militarily conquered by outsiders , and a king needs to be more clever . she also advises him to be kind to his betrothed <SANSA STARK> to avoid stirring up trouble for later , and concludes that anyone who isn't us is an enemy . 
arya and <SANSA STARK> are still at odds over the incident with joffrey and her direwolf . <EDDARD STARK> explains that <SANSA STARK> was put in a difficult position by the king and queen , and while she shouldn't have lied , winning the long term approval of joffrey , her future husband , was important . arya is unhappy with the situation , but <EDDARD STARK> mollifies her by allowing her to practice with her sword , <NEEDLE> . 
 <CATELYN STARK> and <RODRIK CASSEL> arrive in king's <LANDING> . <CATELYN STARK> and ser <RODRIK CASSEL> arrive at king's <LANDING> and attempt to sneak into the city , but are spotted by one of <LITTLEFINGER>'s men . they are taken to meet <LITTLEFINGER> at a brothel he owns , where lord <VARYS> is also waiting one of his'little birds' told him they were coming . <CATELYN STARK> is angered by the way they've been treated , but asks <LITTLEFINGER> for aid in finding the people who tried to have <BRAN STARK> killed . <LITTLEFINGER> is able to answer this quickly the elaborate dagger wielded by the assassin used to be his , but he lost it in a gamble with <TYRION LANNISTER> . 
 <EDDARD STARK> threatens lord baelish . 
 <LITTLEFINGER> fetches <EDDARD STARK> to meet his wife , but <EDDARD STARK> suspects a trick and pushes <LITTLEFINGER> up against a wall <OUTSIDE> the brothel wanting to know what his game is . <CATELYN STARK> then appears , and <EDDARD STARK> is pacified . after hearing her news , he vows to find the truth and expose the <LANNISTERS> to <ROBERT BARATHEON> . <LITTLEFINGER> agrees to be his ally in this , for the affection he once bore <CATELYN STARK> as a youngster . 
ravens arrive at king's <LANDING> with news of <BRAN STARK>'s recovery . cersei fears he will expose their secret , but <JAIME LANNISTER> comforts her . 
 <JAIME LANNISTER> comforts cersei . 
elsewhere , <ROBERT BARATHEON> swaps old war stories with ser <BARRISTAN SELMY> , a distinguished and famous knight and the commander of the <KINGSGUARD> . summoning <JAIME LANNISTER> , <ROBERT BARATHEON> jokingly questions him about <AERYS TARGARYEN>'s death , wondering if the <MAD> king died begging for mercy , but <JAIME LANNISTER> rather coldly replies that the master he betrayed died screaming the same words he'd been saying since the <SIEGE> of king's <LANDING> began burn them all . 
 <EDDARD STARK> has contracted a swordmaster , <SYRIO FOREL> , the former first sword of <BRAAVOS> , to teach arya how to use her sword properly . arya is thrilled , and'the dance' begins . as <EDDARD STARK> watches them practice , his pleasure at seeing arya happy sours when he realizes that a conflict between the <STARKS> and <LANNISTERS> may be inevitable his daughter may well be training herself for war . 
old <NAN> tells <BRAN STARK> of winter and the long knight . 
at winterfell , <BRAN STARK> has awoken but has no memory of his accident . his injuries have left him bedridden and unlikely to walk again . old <NAN> , the oldest servant in the castle , tells <BRAN STARK> stories to pass the time , but he doesn't want her usual heroic stories about the likes of ser duncan the tall . she instead speaks of the <WHITE WALKERS> and the coming of a vast winter that will blanket the world . when robb pays a visit , <BRAN STARK> asks his brother if it is true that his legs are crushed and that he will never walk again . robb reluctantly says this is so . <BRAN STARK> remarks that he would rather be dead . 
at <CASTLE BLACK> , the primary redoubt of the knight's watch in the <SHADOW> of the wall , <JON SNOW> shows his worth to the trainer , ser <ALLISER THORNE> , by besting several fellow members of the watch in the practice yard . <ALLISER THORNE> is disgusted at the poor performance of the others but has no praise for <JON SNOW> either , dubbing him lord <JON SNOW> and describing him as the least useless person here . watching over the new recruits with lord commander <JEOR MORMONT> , <TYRION LANNISTER> notes <ALLISER THORNE>'s stern and unusual ways , but <JEOR MORMONT> doesn't care as he only requires <ALLISER THORNE> to turn the thieves and runaways into men of the knight's watch . later on , several of the other recruits gang up on <JON SNOW> , but the situation is defused by <TYRION LANNISTER> . <TYRION LANNISTER> points out to <JON SNOW> that none of the other recruits had the benefit of a skilled master at arms to train them , and that <JON SNOW> is alienating them through his standoffish attitude and superior combat skills . 
 <BENJEN> talks with <JON SNOW> on the wall . 
 <BENJEN> <BRAN STARK> meets <JON SNOW> atop the wall and tells him he is going on a ranging in the haunted <FOREST> . he refuses to take <JON SNOW> with him , telling him he isn't ready , and that here rank and nobility mean nothing every man must earn everything he gets . before departing , <BENJEN> stops by the eating area to farewell <YOREN> , a fellow knight's watchman who scouts for new recruits in the capital . <BENJEN> also scolds <TYRION LANNISTER> for his naivety regarding what is north of the wall and states that <TYRION LANNISTER> has no authority to say what is or isn't <BEYOND> the wall as he hasn't been out there himself . 
later , <TYRION LANNISTER> discusses north of the wall with <JEOR MORMONT> and his chief adviser , the ancient and blind maester <AEMON> . <JEOR MORMONT> asks for <TYRION LANNISTER> to intercede at court and get the watch more men as they are dangerously undermanned . <AEMON> warns that the <BRAN STARK> words are right a terrible winter is coming and more dangerous things than just <WILDLINGS> might come with it after all , one of their number swore that the <WHITE WALKERS> had returned ... right up to the moment <NED STARK> cut his head off . <TYRION LANNISTER> admits his skepticism that supernatural creatures might exist , but he agrees to bring word to his queen . 
before departing for king's <LANDING> , <TYRION LANNISTER> fulfils an old ambition by climbing to the top of the wall and urinating off the edge of it . he and <JON SNOW> share a moment of fellowship before <TYRION LANNISTER> departs for the capital in the company of <YOREN> .

daenerys rides with the khalasar . 
daenerys commands the khalasar to halt on a whim , exercising her growing authority and power . <VISERYS> does not take well to being commanded and threatens his sister . he is strangled by <RAKHARO> , a dothraki warrior wielding a whip . daenerys calms the situation and <VISERYS> is forced to walk , a sign of shame amongst the horse riding dothraki . later , <IRRI> reveals to daenerys that daenerys is pregnant . daenerys relays the news to <KHAL DROGO> and tells him she thinks it will be a boy as they lie naked in each other's arms . ser <JORAH MORMONT> and <RAKHARO> compare the westerosi and dothraki ways of <BATTLE> the heavily armored but slow knights versus the lightly armored but fast moving horse warriors . <JORAH MORMONT> has heard of <RAKHARO>'s father , a great warrior , but admits that he disgraced his own father , a man of great honor . when he learns that daenerys is pregnant , he announces he must split off from the column to ride to the free city of qohor , but will rejoin them before they reach <VAES DOTHRAK> . 
lord <JON SNOW> is the third episode of the first season of game of thrones . it is the third episode of the series overall . it first aired on may 1 , 2011. it was written by executive producers david benioff d.b . <WEISS> and directed by brian kirk . 
 <JON SNOW> attempts to find his footing at <CASTLE BLACK> amidst hostility and suspicion from his fellow members of the knight's watch . <EDDARD STARK> and his daughters arrive at king's <LANDING> . <CATELYN STARK> renews an old friendship with a member of the court , while daenerys and <VISERYS> journey onwards to the dothraki capital of <VAES DOTHRAK> . 

 <TYRION LANNISTER> speaks with <BRAN STARK> . in winterfell , <BRAN STARK> has a nightmare in which he sees a three eyed raven , sitting on one of the stone direwolves <OUTSIDE> the doorway to the <BRAN STARK> crypts . he wakes up to find his direwolf <SUMMER> by his side . <THEON GREYJOY> summons <HODOR> , the <CASTLE BLACK>'s dim witted stableboy , who can only say the word <HODOR> , to help carry <BRAN STARK> down to the great hall , where <ROBB STARK> is hosting a meeting with <TYRION LANNISTER> and <YOREN> , both traveling down from the wall to king's <LANDING> together . <ROBB STARK> very pointedly offers hospitality to any man of the watch , silently letting <TYRION LANNISTER> know he is not invited to stay at winterfell . 
when <BRAN STARK> arrives , <TYRION LANNISTER> sympathizes with <BRAN STARK> for being a cripple , which annoys <BRAN STARK> , as does asking him if he likes to ride , but <TYRION LANNISTER> simply says it is the truth , no less so for being a hard truth . he gives the <STARKS> the design of a saddle which will allow <BRAN STARK> to ride even in his current state . he does it to repay <BRAN STARK>'s half brother's friendship and because he has a weakness for , <CRIPPLES> , bastards and broken things . due to this kindness , <ROBB STARK> says he can stay , but <TYRION LANNISTER> says he would prefer the brothel in <TOWN> . while preparing to leave the <CASTLE BLACK> , <THEON GREYJOY> comes to <TYRION LANNISTER> and rather condescendingly sends him off , recommending the prostitute ros at the brothel . <TYRION LANNISTER> asks <THEON GREYJOY> why lady <CATELYN STARK> was not present to receive him and concludes that <CATELYN STARK> is not in winterfell . he also taunts <THEON GREYJOY> about how the son of the ferocious <BALON GREYJOY> has been reduced to playing lackey in winterfell to his captors , which infuriates <THEON GREYJOY> and gives him a coin , assuming that he has not already had sex with ros . 
 <SAMWELL TARLY> joins the new recruits at <CASTLE BLACK> . 
at <CASTLE BLACK> , a new recruit for the knight's watch has arrived <SAMWELL TARLY> , the son of the famous lord randyll <SAMWELL TARLY> . <SAMWELL TARLY> is fat , soft and pampered , and in his first practice fight does dismally . ser <ALLISER THORNE> has no time for his weakness . he directs the other recruits to attack'ser <PIGGY>' , but <JON SNOW> finds this cruel and unfair , and takes pity on <SAM> and fends off the attackers . <ALLISER THORNE> tries to turn it into a game , ordering three trainees take on <SAM>'s <PROTECTOR> taunting <JON SNOW> that he has found a new lady love , but <JON SNOW> nevertheless fends them all off . <SAMWELL TARLY> is naive and self deprecating , claiming to be a coward and craven , to <JON SNOW>'s astonishment . no one admits to being a coward , and <GRENN> says that they shouldn't even be seen talking to him . 
 <SAM> joins <JON SNOW> on the wall for sentry duty , even though he says his eyesight is weak , he is afraid of heights , and can't take the cold . <JON SNOW> asks why he joined the knight's watch as he is afraid of everything . <SAM> tells him that on his eighteenth nameday his father offered him a choice . <SAM> was a man and his heir , but he was not skilled at combat , he was unworthy of his name and birthright . samwall's father forced him to join the knight's watch , and told him that if he refused , he would arrange a hunting trip with his son in the woods , and implied that <SAM> would be killed in a way that looked accidental . <JON SNOW> is shocked that a true born son of high birth should be treated worse than he himself had been as a bastard . <SAM> knows that the next day he will be made to fight again and expects it to be bad . 
 <GRENN> yields to <SAMWELL TARLY> . at the wall , <JON SNOW> orders the recruits to go easy on <SAM> , but <RAST> refuses , saying that if ser <ALLISER THORNE> orders him to fight'lady <PIGGY>' , he will slice himself off a side of bacon . in response to <RAST>'s comments , <JON SNOW> goes to his bed that knight and uses his direwolf ghost to intimidate <RAST> into playing along . the next day , no one will fight <SAM> . after <GRENN> takes a very weak blow from <SAM> and yields , ser <ALLISER THORNE> scolds <JON SNOW> for his rebellious actions . later , when <JON SNOW> and <SAM> are cleaning the dining hall , they talk about how neither of them have been with a woman . <SAM> tells <JON SNOW> that he has not had success with girls , while <JON SNOW> reveals he'd rather not risk siring a child that will have the life of a bastard like himself . a furious <ALLISER THORNE> comes in and tells <JON SNOW> that this charity won't help <SAM> harden up to survive the winter that is coming . he tells them the truly horrific experience he went through trapped by a blizzard north of the wall that ended in cannibalism . 
a . 
 <KHAL DROGO>'s khalasar arrives at <VAES DOTHRAK> , the dothraki city . there are no city walls , but there is a large gateway arch made of two statues of rearing horses . <VISERYS> is annoyed that <KHAL DROGO> has been taking'his' <ARMY> in the wrong direction . later , he bathes with <DOREAH> and tells her about how he was raised with stories about the targaryen dragons and his own destiny . he recites the names of several dragons , and tells her about the skulls of dragons that once decorated the throne room at king's <LANDING> , but she starts to annoy him with talk of dragons , reminding him that they are dead . he tells her to finish pleasuring him in silence . 
 <VISERYS> is enraged when daenerys sends <DOREAH> with an invite for him to dine with her , as he interprets this as his sister commanding him to come . he drags <DOREAH> into daenerys' tent , and insults her dinner and the gifts of clothes she tries to give him . he is still dressed in his now ragged clothes from <PENTOS> , having refused to dress like a dothraki , whom he regards as savage pordh . he sneers that next she will try to braid his hair like a dothraki . daenerys retorts that he has no right to braid his hair until he is victorious in <BATTLE> , which further infuriates him . in his anger , <VISERYS> tackles her to the ground and tries to strike her , calling her nothing but a horselord's slut , and warning her that she's awoken the dragon , but this time she fights back , hitting him in the face with a metal and leather belt . she tells a thunderstruck <VISERYS> that she is the <KHAL DROGO>'s wife , and is carrying his child and by implication , <VISERYS> is nothing to the dothraki , and warns that if he raises a <HAND> against her again , he will lose his hands . later , daenerys confides in mormont her realization that <VISERYS> will never become king of <WESTEROS> . he is so weak and ineffectual that he couldn't command an <ARMY> even if <KHAL DROGO> gave him one , to which jorah agrees . 
in the <RED KEEP> , <SANSA STARK> visits the great hall , where the <IRON THRONE> sits . she and <SEPTA MORDANE> discuss the expectation that <SANSA STARK> will have to provide joffrey with an heir . <SANSA STARK> thinks the <REALM> will hate her if she only has daughters , along with her belief joffrey is still angry over the incident by the river and her anger at her father over lady's death . 
the <SMALL COUNCIL> meets . during a meeting of the <SMALL COUNCIL> , lord eddard learns that the forthcoming tournament to celebrate his appointment is seeing the city swell with visitors , and has already resulted in a tavern riot , a brothel fire , three stabbings and a drunken horse race . he tells <LITTLEFINGER> that money will have to be found to strengthen the city guards , as well as giving twenty of his own men to <JANOS SLYNT>'s command , until the tournament is over . after the meeting eddard talks to <GRAND> maester <PYCELLE> about <JON ARRYN>'s last few weeks . <PYCELLE> said he did all he could to save <JON ARRYN> , but the illness was sudden and severe . he recalls that shortly before his sudden illness , <JON ARRYN> had borrowed a truly boring book about the lineages of the <SEVEN KINGDOMS> , and his last words were , the seed is strong . 
taking the book with him , eddard comes across arya in the hall standing on one leg as part of her training with syrio . arya asks whether <BRAN STARK> would be able to live in king's <LANDING> with them now that he's awoken , but eddard states that he would have to regain his strength first . arya then comments that <BRAN STARK> had always wanted to be a knight in the king's guard , but will no longer be able to due to his paralysis . eddard confirms this to be the case , but states that <BRAN STARK> will be able to do many other things such as become lord of a holdfast , sit on the king's <SMALL COUNCIL> , or raise castles . when arya asks if she would be able to become any of those , eddard instead tells her that she will marry a highborn lord and have lords and princes for sons . however , arya is not pleased with this response , telling her father , that's not me . she goes back to balancing on one leg as eddard looks on . 
 <PETYR> talks with eddard . <LITTLEFINGER> meets with eddard and suggests that he <RED KEEP> his investigation into <JON ARRYN>'s death lower in profile . he also gives eddard some interesting intelligence <JON ARRYN>'s former squire has been knighted and will fight in the forthcoming <HAND>'s tourney . he also advises him to investigate an armorer located in the city . eddard decides that <LITTLEFINGER> may be more trustworthy than he first thought , but <LITTLEFINGER> discourages him from thinking that way . eddard sends <JORY CASSEL> to question <JON ARRYN>'s former squire , ser <HUGH> of the <VALE> . however , deducing that <JORY CASSEL> was not a knight , ser <HUGH> simply rebuffs him and refuses to speak with him due to his much lower rank . eddard's investigation leads him to a smithy in the city , where he meets master smith tobho mott and his apprentice <GENDRY> , whose work <JON ARRYN> was also apparently interested in . eddard realizes that <GENDRY> is one of king robert's bastard sons , but can't work out why <JON ARRYN> would be interested in this robert has many bastard children and shows little interest in any of them . 
later , eddard sends <JORY CASSEL> with a message for king robert , but upon arriving at his quarters , the sounds of many women can he heard coming from robert's chamber . ser <JAIME LANNISTER> happens to be on duty and is angry that the king keeps him guarding his chamber while he cavorts with other women inside , flaunting his dishonorable treatment of <JAIME LANNISTER>'s sister in his face . he and <JORY CASSEL> reminisce about the greyjoy <REBELLION> , in which they both fought for king robert's forces to put down an attempt by <BALON GREYJOY> theon's father to secede the <IRON ISLANDS> from the rest of the <REALM> . <JORY CASSEL> tries to leave eddard's message with <JAIME LANNISTER> , but is rebuffed , as <JAIME LANNISTER> angrily states that he does not serve lord <BRAN STARK> . <LITTLEFINGER> , arya , <SANSA STARK> and <SEPTA MORDANE> at the tournament . the tournament begins and <SANSA STARK> watches from the stands . ser <GREGOR CLEGANE> , the elder brother of <SANDOR CLEGANE> , the <HOUND> , takes the field . his first joust is with ser <HUGH> . however , the friendly joust turns nasty and <GREGOR CLEGANE> kills ser <HUGH> by accident , with a splinter of the lance impaling his <NECK> . <LITTLEFINGER> sits next to <SANSA STARK> , and remarks that she and joffrey have had a lover's quarrel as joffrey is still giving her the cold shoulder . baelish then tells <SANSA STARK> that <GREGOR CLEGANE> , the mountain that rides , has a dark reputation he pushed his little brother <SANDOR CLEGANE>'s face into a fire for taking and playing with a toy of his when they were young , burning him severely . <LITTLEFINGER> recommends that <SANSA STARK> not spread that story around . 
cersei visits eddard at his chambers , remarking at how the <HAND> is not at his own tournament . though cersei attempts to start the conversation in an attempt to put the incident on the <KINGSROAD> behind them , eddard correctly deduces that she has an ulterior motive for her visit . cersei then wonders aloud to eddard what his true purpose is for being at king's <LANDING> , as she knows how little <STARKS> enjoy being in the capital . when eddard tells her he is to faithfully serve their king , cersei remarks that as his brother brandon was born to lead , eddard was born to follow . 
at the <CROSSROADS INN> , catelyn and ser <RODRIK CASSEL> , on their way <HOME> to winterfell , are enjoying the hospitality of the innkeeper and , more reluctantly , the attempts by the troubadour <MARILLION> to ingratiate himself with them . he is doing a poor job when he asks if they would like a song , he is refused . they are surprised when <TYRION LANNISTER> and <YOREN> arrive . when told there aren't any rooms , <TYRION LANNISTER> holds up a gold coin and asks if someone has a room for him . quickly <TYRION LANNISTER> gains the favor of a sellsword , bronn , who agrees to give his room to <TYRION LANNISTER> . <MARILLION> draws the attention of <TYRION LANNISTER> to catelyn's table , by offering to serenade him while he eats , singing of his father's military victories . <TYRION LANNISTER> says nothing would more likely ruin his appetite , but as he is turning away , he recognizes catelyn and is surprised at this meeting by chance . in return catelyn tells the stunned <CROSSROADS INN> that <TYRION LANNISTER> tried to murder her son <BRAN STARK> twice and that she asks their help in bringing him to the king's justice . the <CROSSROADS INN> is located in the <RIVERLANDS> , in the territory controlled by her father , so the knights present owe him their fealty . <TYRION LANNISTER> finds himself surrounded by half a dozen men with swords , and in catelyn's custody . 
 <CRIPPLES> , bastards and broken things is the fourth episode of the first season . 
 <TYRION LANNISTER> stops at winterfell on his way back to king's <LANDING> and gets a frosty reception from <ROBB STARK> , despite an act of kindness for <BRAN STARK> . <SAMWELL TARLY> joins the knight's watch , and <JON ARRYN> becomes his friend and <PROTECTOR> . daenerys arrives at <VAES DOTHRAK> and finally stands up to <VISERYS> . <EDDARD STARK> continues to investigate the death of <JON ARRYN> . king <ROBERT BARATHEON> hosts a <GRAND> tourney for <EDDARD STARK>'s investiture as <HAND> of the king , to ned's discomfort . catelyn and ser <RODRIK CASSEL> stop at the <CROSSROADS INN> . 

 <TYRION LANNISTER> and his escorts in the hills of the <VALE> . 
 <TYRION LANNISTER> has his blindfold removed and finds that their party augmented by several knights and the sellsword bronn from the <CROSSROADS INN> is on the eastern road en route to the <VALE> of <JON ARRYN> . catelyn notes that she said they were riding for winterfell often and loudly . <TYRION LANNISTER> congratulates her on her cunning , while pointing out that his father will give out a handsome reward for his safe return a point that clearly piques bronn's interest . he also says that lady <LYSA ARRYN> has gone <MAD> since her husband's death and will try to kill him in the <EYRIE> . <TYRION LANNISTER> also protests his innocence in the attempt on <BRAN STARK>'s life and points out he'd have to be an idiot to give the assassin his own blade . before catelyn can answer , the party comes under attack from one of the hill tribes . despite taking several losses , the party is able to drive off the attackers . despite having the opportunity to escape , <TYRION LANNISTER> fights , killing his first man during the skirmish , and in doing so saves catelyn's life . afterwards , they resume their trek to the <EYRIE> . 
 <TYRION LANNISTER> and catelyn in the <EYRIE>'s <HIGH HALL> . 
in the <HIGH HALL> of the <EYRIE> , lady <LYSA ARRYN> holds court on behalf of her young son , <ROBIN> . <LYSA ARRYN> is furious that <CAT> has endangered them all by bringing <TYRION LANNISTER> to the <VALE> . <TYRION LANNISTER> points out that if he is harmed , there will be war with <HOUSE LANNISTER> , but <LYSA ARRYN> is unconcerned about his threats , as the <VALE> is strongly defended and the <EYRIE> is impregnable . she orders him sent to the sky cells , three sided cells with the fourth open to a sheer drop down the mountainside , forcing <TYRION LANNISTER> to huddle in a corner and try not to roll out to his death in his sleep . 
in winterfell , <BRAN STARK> is angry about his mother's absence . maester <LUWIN> tries to set his mind at rest about the matter , to no avail . however , when <BRAN STARK> gets frustrated at not being able to practice his archery , <LUWIN> suggests that he could learn to use a shortbow , of the kind used in mounted combat by the dothraki , a notion which pleases <BRAN STARK> . . 
 <BRAN STARK> and maester <LUWIN> discuss geography . 
elsewhere in the castle , <THEON GREYJOY> enjoys the attentions of his favorite whore , ros , but becomes annoyed when she compares his prowess unfavorably to that of <TYRION LANNISTER> . 
lord <EDDARD STARK> arrives at the tourney ground to speak to lord commander <BARRISTAN SELMY> about the death of ser <HUGH> of the <VALE> . <BARRISTAN SELMY> notes that he had no family or friends so he stood the knight's vigil himself for ser <HUGH> . <EDDARD STARK> is suspicious of ser <HUGH>'s death , wanting to know how he could afford a new set of armor so soon after being made a knight . <BARRISTAN SELMY> reflects on the irony of them being on opposite sides of the war during <ROBERT BARATHEON>'s <REBELLION> and now they are working together . . 
ser <BARRISTAN SELMY> and lord <EDDARD STARK> discuss the death of ser <HUGH> . 
he also tells <EDDARD STARK> that king <ROBERT BARATHEON> is planning to joust during the day's activities . <EDDARD STARK> finds king <ROBERT BARATHEON> tormenting his squire , <LANCEL LANNISTER> , finally sending him off on a snipe hunt in amused disgust . <ROBERT BARATHEON> is adamant about fighting in the joust but <EDDARD STARK> tells him that he is too fat for his armor and the other knights would let him <LUWIN> . <ROBERT BARATHEON> is forced to admit that he's right but they can at least watch the joust from the stands . 
the first tilt of the day is between the fearsome ser <GREGOR CLEGANE> , the mountain , and the popular'knight of the flowers' , ser <LORAS> tyrell . <LORAS> gives a beautiful flower to <SANSA STARK> , while <LITTLEFINGER> and lord <RENLY> make a wager on who will <LUWIN> with <RENLY> betting on <LORAS> . <LORAS> is riding a mare that is in heat , which confuses the mountain's horse , causing him to throw his rider . . 
king <ROBERT BARATHEON> is dismayed to find he no longer fits his armor . 
enraged at having lost , <GREGOR CLEGANE> first decapitates his horse and then attacks ser <LORAS> . <SANDOR CLEGANE> comes to <LORAS>' defense , preventing his brother from killing him . they exchange several blows , until king <ROBERT BARATHEON> orders them to cease . <SANDOR CLEGANE> immediately bows to the king , while <GREGOR CLEGANE> storms off the field . ser <LORAS> declares <SANDOR CLEGANE> the victor of the match to the <HOUND>'s discomfort . 
in the <RED KEEP> , lord <VARYS> meets with <EDDARD STARK> . <VARYS> tells him that the king is a fool and will soon be dead unless <EDDARD STARK> can save him . <EDDARD STARK> wants to know why <VARYS> is telling him this now . <VARYS> tells him he had to be sure <EDDARD STARK> could be trusted . 
he calls <EDDARD STARK> an honorable and true man , maybe the only one in the city . he also confirms that <JON ARRYN> was assassinated with a poison called the tears of <LYS> because he started asking questions . arya is chasing cats in accordance with her sword training . she chases one into the dungeons under the castle , where she finds the great dragon skulls of the <TARGARYENS> in storage . she hears two men <VARYS> and magister <ILLYRIO> mopatis of <PENTOS> talking . <VARYS> says that events have been set in motion and the <REBELLION> and the wolf will soon be at each other's throats . war is almost upon the <SEVEN KINGDOMS> , as they planned , but it has come too soon . <KHAL DROGO> will not invade <WESTEROS> until his son is born and pronounced healthy , which is still many months away . <ILLYRIO> suggests assassinating <EDDARD STARK> to forestall the war , but <VARYS> refuses . 
 <SANDOR CLEGANE> , ser <GREGOR CLEGANE> and ser <LORAS> at the tournament . 
afterwards , <VARYS> finds <LITTLEFINGER> in the great <HIGH HALL> staring at the <IRON THRONE> . <VARYS> reveals that he knows about <LITTLEFINGER>'s assistance in <EDDARD STARK>'s investigation of <JON ARRYN>'s death and reminds <LITTLEFINGER> of the consequences that may befall him should the <LANNISTERS> discover his involvement . in response , <LITTLEFINGER> reveals that he already knows about <VARYS> having met with both <EDDARD STARK> and <ILLYRIO> just earlier that day , implying he knows of <VARYS>' allegiances across the <NARROW SEA> . their conversation is interrupted by <RENLY> , who informs them that <ROBERT BARATHEON> will be joining them at their <SMALL COUNCIL> meeting . 
arya escapes from the dungeon and tries to warn her father about what she overheard but she gets the words muddled up . they are interrupted by <YOREN> , who has ridden non stop from the <CROSSROADS INN> to bring <EDDARD STARK> forewarning of catelyn's arrest of <TYRION LANNISTER> . <EDDARD STARK> keeps the information to himself , while arya asks <JORY CASSEL> about the state of her father's household guard . <JORY CASSEL> tells her she does not have to worry about her father's safety . 
at the meeting of the <SMALL COUNCIL> , king <ROBERT BARATHEON> tells <EDDARD STARK> that <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> is pregnant and her son will have a claim to the <IRON THRONE> . he wants <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> , the unborn child , and <VISERYS> dead as soon as possible . . 
 <VARYS> secretly meets <ILLYRIO> under the <RED KEEP> . 
 <EDDARD STARK> states that this act would be dishonorable , cowardly , and beneath their dignity . the other members of the <SMALL COUNCIL> <PYCELLE> , <RENLY> , <LITTLEFINGER> and <VARYS> all concur that <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> must die for the good of the <REALM> . king <ROBERT BARATHEON> orders <EDDARD STARK> to enact the order . he refuses and resigns as the <HAND> of the king , to <ROBERT BARATHEON>'s utter disbelief and fury . 
 <EDDARD STARK> orders his household to begin packing . as <EDDARD STARK> is packing , <LITTLEFINGER> arrives and offers to take <EDDARD STARK> to the last place <JON ARRYN> went before he fell ill . <EDDARD STARK> agrees . 
ser <LORAS> and lord <RENLY> , who are lovers , meet in a bedchamber . <RENLY> complains as <ROBERT BARATHEON> is organizing a hunt in the kingswood , which will no doubt involve traipsing around the <FOREST> for a couple of weeks in the cold and rain waiting to kill some animal . <LORAS> urges <RENLY> to claim the crown himself , offering him the allegiance of his rich and powerful family . <RENLY> dismisses the notion , since he is fourth in line to the <IRON THRONE> . <LORAS> points out that joffrey is a monster , that <TOMMEN> is only eight and laughs at the notion of <ROBERT BARATHEON> and <RENLY>'s other brother , lord stannis , ever becoming king , as he has the charisma and personality of a lobster . he also asserts that the people love <RENLY> and want to serve him because he is kind and doesn't revel in violence as his <BROTHERS> do . 
queen cersei and <ROBERT BARATHEON> share a rare drink and discussion about the <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> threat . surprisingly , cersei takes <EDDARD STARK>'s side , pointing out that the dothraki can not cross the <NARROW SEA> as they have no ships . . 
ser <LORAS> urges <RENLY> to consider his place in the line of succession . 
 <ROBERT BARATHEON> agrees , but if they land and the knights of <WESTEROS> take shelter behind their castle walls , the dothraki could simply burn and pillage their way up and down the continent until the smallfolk accept <VISERYS> as their king regardless . cersei suggests that the unified armies of the <SEVEN KINGDOMS> could defeat them but <ROBERT BARATHEON> says she underestimates the skill and ability of one <ARMY> with one leader and one purpose as compared to that of the scattered and patchwork armies of <WESTEROS> . their discussion moves to <LYANNA STARK> , which surprises <ROBERT BARATHEON> , as in seventeen years cersei has never asked about her . he tells her that <LYANNA STARK>'s death left in him a void that <SEVEN KINGDOMS> could not fill . he also tells her that their marriage never had a chance of success because of the <HOLD> <LYANNA STARK>'s memory has on him , and bitterly adds he can barely remember what she looked like . cersei says that she felt something for <ROBERT BARATHEON> once , even after they lost their first boy , for quite a while . she asks <ROBERT BARATHEON> if there was ever any chance for their marriage and he answers no . 
 <LITTLEFINGER> brings <EDDARD STARK> to the last place <JON ARRYN> went before falling ill , which is one of littefinger's brothels . there <EDDARD STARK> meets another one of <ROBERT BARATHEON>'s bastards , this time a girl , and her mother , a blond whore named <MHAEGEN> . <MHAEGEN> remarks that her child has <ROBERT BARATHEON>'s nose and black hair . <EDDARD STARK> asks <LITTLEFINGER> why <JON ARRYN> was searching for <ROBERT BARATHEON>'s bastards but he says he doesn't know , offering the half hearted guess that maybe <ROBERT BARATHEON> suddenly took paternal interest in them . <EDDARD STARK> looks skeptical of that reason . 
leaving the brothel , <EDDARD STARK> , <JORY CASSEL> , and the two guards that accompanied them are confronted by a large group of <TYRION LANNISTER> guardsmen led by ser <JAIME LANNISTER> . <JAIME LANNISTER> has heard of <TYRION LANNISTER>'s arrest and demands an explanation . <EDDARD STARK> says that <TYRION LANNISTER> was arrested on his orders . . 
 <EDDARD STARK> is stabbed through the leg by a <TYRION LANNISTER> guardsman . 
 <JAIME LANNISTER> threatens to kill <EDDARD STARK> but <EDDARD STARK> points out that if he does , <TYRION LANNISTER> will die as well . <JAIME LANNISTER> acknowledges that this is true , so he says he will settle for killing <EDDARD STARK>'s <TOMMEN> instead . there is a brief engagement in which <EDDARD STARK>'s two guards , heward and wyl , are killed by <JAIME LANNISTER> spearmen . in response , ned and <JORY CASSEL> fight and kill five of the <JAIME LANNISTER> soldiers . <JORY CASSEL> engages <JAIME LANNISTER> but is quickly killed when <JAIME LANNISTER> stabs him through the eye with a dagger . furious , <EDDARD STARK> crosses swords with <JAIME LANNISTER> . <JAIME LANNISTER> is shocked and then exhilarated when the older ned is not as easily defeated as he expected . however , <JAIME LANNISTER> gradually starts to grow worried as ned's <HIGH HALL> level of skill becomes apparent . just as they are ready to clash again , a <JAIME LANNISTER> guardsman steps in and stabs <EDDARD STARK> through the leg with a spear , disabling him . <JAIME LANNISTER> is annoyed at the dishonorable interruption and knocks out the guardsman . he departs , telling <EDDARD STARK> he wants his brother back . 
the wolf and the lion is the fifth episode of the first season of game of thrones and the fifth episode of the series overall . it first aired on may 15 , 2011. it was written by executive producers david benioff d.b . <WEISS> and directed by brian kirk . 
 <TYRION LANNISTER>'s predicament becomes common knowledge in king's <LANDING> , making life difficult for <EDDARD STARK> . ned's position is already precarious due to a disagreement with king <ROBERT BARATHEON> over plans to assassinate <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> before she can rally the dothraki to invade <WESTEROS> . in the <EYRIE> , catelyn is shocked by her sister lysa's paranoia and distrust . 

lord <EDDARD STARK> wakes up after a long period of unconsciousness , due to the injuries inflicted on him by <JAIME LANNISTER>'s <TOMMEN> . he finds both king <ROBERT BARATHEON> and queen cersei waiting . . 
king <ROBERT BARATHEON>'s hunting party . 
cersei is furious with <EDDARD STARK>'s acts in having her brother <TYRION LANNISTER> arrested and attacking <JAIME LANNISTER> in the street . she wants <ROBERT BARATHEON> to take action against him , but <ROBERT BARATHEON> refuses to condemn him without hearing <EDDARD STARK>'s side , and tells her to be silent . when cersei protests further , and calls <ROBERT BARATHEON> a woman , he hits her . she says that she will wear the bruise with honor . he tells her to be silent , or he will honor her again , and cersei leaves in anger . afterwards , <ROBERT BARATHEON> restores <EDDARD STARK> to his position as king's <HAND> , and tells him not to quit again , or he will give the position to <JAIME LANNISTER> . he tells lord <EDDARD STARK> to end the animosity between <HOUSE STARK> and <HOUSE LANNISTER> , as strife between these two powerful houses could lead them into war . he is leaving on a hunt and wants the <REALM> at peace by the time he returns . 
arya has another dancing lesson with <SYRIO FOREL> , but isn't in the mood due to <JORY CASSEL>'s death . <SYRIO FOREL> tells her that she may need to fight at any time , not just when she's in the mood . he wisely reminds her that being prepared to fight is more important in times of sadness than in peaceful times of happiness . 
king <ROBERT BARATHEON> is out hunting , accompanied by his brother <RENLY> , ser <BARRISTAN SELMY> and <LANCEL LANNISTER> . <ROBERT BARATHEON> , being supplied with wine by <LANCEL LANNISTER> , becomes drunk and nostalgic , longing for the days of young knights trying to make a name for themselves and when enemies stood openly in opposition instead of being hidden schemers . <ROBERT BARATHEON> brags about all the women he has bedded , but <RENLY> becomes irate when he begins to question him about his history with women . <RENLY> calls him a fool and remarks that the past had its share of violence that <ROBERT BARATHEON> is conveniently ignoring . <RENLY> storms off , leaving ser <BARRISTAN SELMY> to look on concerned , as <LANCEL LANNISTER> keeps up king <ROBERT BARATHEON>'s wine supply . 
in king's <LANDING> , at a meeting of the <SMALL COUNCIL> , a group of refugees come to tell of how their villages have been destroyed . <EDDARD STARK> hears tales of a huge knight ravaging the <RIVERLANDS> . he realizes that it's ser <GREGOR CLEGANE> , the mountain , who is likely under <LANCEL LANNISTER> orders to punish the <RIVERLANDS> which are held by <HOUSE TULLY> , the former <HOUSE TULLY> of his wife catelyn , who now holds <TYRION LANNISTER> captive . even though king <ROBERT BARATHEON> told him to make peace with the <LANNISTERS> , lord <EDDARD STARK> could not bring himself to let this injustice stand . <EDDARD STARK> strips <GREGOR CLEGANE> of his knighthood , land , and titles , and sends lord <BERIC> <DONDARRION> with a retinue of one hundred knights to arrest and execute him in the king's name . . 
 <EDDARD STARK> discovers the secret <JON ARRYN> died for . 
he also orders <GRAND> maester <PYCELLE> to send word to <CASTERLY ROCK> , demanding lord <TYWIN LANNISTER>'s presence in court to explain his bannerman's actions or be branded an enemy of the crown and a traitor to the <REALM> .'littlefinger' <PETYR> baelish , and <GRAND> maester <PYCELLE> are both concerned with the harshness of these orders and <EDDARD STARK>'s actions against the <LANNISTERS> , but <EDDARD STARK> wants to see justice done . 
prince joffrey comes to apologize to sansa for the incident on the <KINGSROAD> . he calls her his lady love and gives her a necklace . sansa forgives him , and they seem reconciled . sansa is unaware that the queen put joffrey up to the apology some time ago . 
 <EDDARD STARK> decides to send his daughters back to winterfell . arya is worried that she must leave <SYRIO FOREL> . sansa protests that no one cares about her trivial dancing instructor , they are talking about breaking her betrothal to joffrey . lord <EDDARD STARK> says that he will find someone else for her . sansa refuses she is going to marry joffrey and have lots of golden haired babies . this gives <EDDARD STARK> pause and sends him back to the book that <JON ARRYN> was looking at before he died . consulting the book's entry on <HOUSE BARATHEON> , lord <EDDARD STARK> finds that every time a <HOUSE BARATHEON> has married , the children have had black hair right up to cersei and <ROBERT BARATHEON>'s children , who are all blond . 
stiv and <OSHA> accost bran near winterfell . 
in winterfell , bran has another dream about the three eyed raven , in which it flies into the castle's crypts . he wakes up to find that <HODOR> has brought the finished saddle designed by <TYRION LANNISTER> . he goes on a ride with robb and <ROBERT BARATHEON> . they have had word from king's <LANDING> about <EDDARD STARK>'s injury , <JORY CASSEL>'s death and <TYRION LANNISTER>'s capture . <ROBERT BARATHEON> thinks that robb should prepare the north for war , but robb is determined to make his own decision for when that time has come , and until then will follow his parents' orders to remain in winterfell . they discover that bran has wandered off on his horse and go looking for him . robb finds a group of <WILDLINGS> threatening bran and trying to steal his horse . robb kills two , but another wildling holds bran with a knife to the throat . <ROBERT BARATHEON> shoots him from behind , angering robb by endangering bran . the remaining wildling , a woman named <OSHA> , yields and begs for her life . robb agrees to take her as a prisoner . 
 <ROBERT BARATHEON> tells ros he will miss her as she leaves for king's <LANDING> . 
ros , the prostitute that <ROBERT BARATHEON> frequently sees , is departing winterfell for king's <LANDING> on the back of a turnip cart . <ROBERT BARATHEON> stops her and unsuccessfully tries to persuade her to stay . she explains that war is now imminent and the <TOMMEN> and thus her customer base of winterfell are destined to leave soon and probably never return her departure is thus an economically essential decision . he throws her a coin to get her to raise her skirt one last time . as she rides off he says that he will miss her . she agrees that he will . <TYRION LANNISTER>'s verbal skills are wasted on mord . 
at the <EYRIE> , <TYRION LANNISTER> almost rolls out of his sky cell in his sleep , to his consternation . he tries to make a bargain with the gaoler , mord , to no avail . 
 <TYRION LANNISTER> convinces mord to carry a message to lady <LYSA ARRYN> and , in exchange , he will give mord the gold he had with him when he was captured . <LYSA ARRYN> summons <TYRION LANNISTER> , believing that the sky cell has broken his spirit , but all he confesses to is being a liar , a whoremonger , and a player of practical jokes . he maintains his innocence of the crimes of conspiracy to commit murder . 
 <TYRION LANNISTER> on trial in the <EYRIE> . 
however , <TYRION LANNISTER> uses the opportunity of his audience in front of <LYSA ARRYN>'s court to publicly demand his right to justice and a trial , and <LYSA ARRYN> is shamed into agreeing . given that <LYSA ARRYN>'s son is a young boy and wouldn't make a good judge in a formal trial , <TYRION LANNISTER> instead demands a trial by combat , which <LYSA ARRYN> also reluctantly agrees is his right . given that neither <LYSA ARRYN> nor her young son can fight in a trial by combat , she asks for a volunteer to be her champion , and ser <VARDIS EGEN> agrees . <VARDIS EGEN> is unwilling to fight <TYRION LANNISTER> however , as killing such an outmatched opponent would be dishonourable . <TYRION LANNISTER> names his own champion his brother <JAIME LANNISTER> , considered one of the best swordsmen in the <REALM> . at this <LYSA ARRYN> does object , as <JAIME LANNISTER> is not present and she does not want to wait . she demands that he pick a champion from those present . <TYRION LANNISTER> desperately asks for volunteers , and after a long pause during which it seems that <TYRION LANNISTER>'s cause is lost , the sellsword bronn steps forward and says he will stand for him . bronn kicks ser <VARDIS EGEN>'s corpse out of the <MOON DOOR> . 
bronn fights defensively , waiting for <VARDIS EGEN> to tire , as unlike bronn he is dressed in full armor . bronn finally gets his chance he first wounds and then kills <VARDIS EGEN> , sending his body rolling out of the <MOON DOOR> that leads to a thousand foot drop . <LYSA ARRYN> complains that bronn did not fight with honor . bronn agrees , but indicates that <VARDIS EGEN> did fight with honor . <TYRION LANNISTER> has proven his innocence in the eyes of the gods . he retrieves his gold from ser rodrik and gives it to mord . when <ROBIN> asks if he can make the little woman fly now , <TYRION LANNISTER> says , this little woman is going <HOME> . bronn and <TYRION LANNISTER> are allowed to depart .

 <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> is summoned by the crones who rule the city , the <DOSH KHALEEN> , the wives of khals slain in <BATTLE> . she eats a stallion's heart and the crones read the omens . at first it seems <DANY> won't keep the raw meat down , but , to both her and drogo's relief , she is able to compose herself . the crones declare <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> and drogo's son will be the stallion that mounts the world , a great conqueror whose coming is long foretold in dothraki history . <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> says his name will be <RHAEGO> , for her brother rhaegar , slain by the usurper <ROBERT BARATHEON> . <VISERYS> is not impressed and rather disgusted by it all . he stands with ser jorah who explains the ritual to him . it is only when the dothraki are chanting <RHAEGO>'s name , and drogo lifts <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> up and carries her about the room , that <VISERYS> realizes they love her . .

 <KHAL DROGO> gives <VISERYS> a golden crown .
