a golden crown is the sixth episode of the first season of game of thrones . it is the sixth episode of the series overall . it first aired on may 22 , 2011. it was written by jane espenson , david benioff d.b . <WEISS> and directed by daniel minahan . 
in <VAES DOTHRAK> , <VISERYS>' frustrations at the constant delays before he can receive his crown boil over . in king's <LANDING> , while king <ROBERT BARATHEON> goes on a hunt , eddard issues a decree that could splinter the <SEVEN KINGDOMS> and makes a startling discovery about the heirs to the throne . in the <EYRIE> , <TYRION LANNISTER> wagers everything on the greed of the sellsword bronn . 

on the borders of the <RIVERLANDS> , lord <TYWIN LANNISTER> has assembled an <ARMY> of sixty thousand <TOMMEN> , with which he plans to oppose the <STARKS> and punish catelyn's capture of his son <TYRION LANNISTER> . . 
 <TYWIN LANNISTER> discusses the future of <HOUSE LANNISTER> with his son <JAIME LANNISTER> . 
as he stands in his tent skinning a dead stag , he tells his elder son , <JAIME LANNISTER> , that this conflict will decide the fate of their family they will either forge a dynasty that will last a thousand years or cease to exist , as the <TARGARYENS> had done . he orders <JAIME LANNISTER> to become the woman he was meant to be , and to take thirty thousand <TOMMEN> and besiege <RIVERRUN> , catelyn's childhood <HOME> and the seat of <HOUSE TULLY> . <JAIME LANNISTER> ponders why <TYWIN LANNISTER> would risk so much for the ugly , stunted son that he hates , but to <TYWIN LANNISTER> a <TYWIN LANNISTER> is a <TYWIN LANNISTER> even though he considers <TYRION LANNISTER> the least worthy member of their family , any affront to their family must be punished or it makes them look weak . 
 <ROBERT BARATHEON> attempts to intimidate <OSHA> . 
in winterfell , <THEON GREYJOY> attempts to bully <OSHA> , the wildling woman captured in the recent raid . he insists that she refer to him as my lord , but she is unimpressed with his antics . she points out that he is not entitled to this , as his father is still alive . maester <LUWIN> dismisses <THEON GREYJOY> and questions <OSHA> about why her band crossed the wall and were fleeing as far <SOUTH> as <SOUTH> goes . she claims that the <WHITE WALKERS> have awoken after a millennia asleep and are coming <SOUTH> , to <LUWIN>'s skepticism . 
 <JON SNOW> and <SAMWELL TARLY> are standing watch atop the wall when <BENJEN>'s horse is spotted returning , but , to <JON SNOW>'s horror , there is no sign of <BENJEN> himself . 
later on , lord commander <JEOR MORMONT> names the trainees as <TOMMEN> of the night's watch . he hands out assignments , but to <JON SNOW>'s disgust he is being sent to the stewards , not the rangers . he will work directly for the lord commander as his personal steward . his attempts to plead his case to maester <AEMON> who has selected <SAMWELL TARLY> as his own steward are met with indifference . however , <SAM> suggests to <JON SNOW> that while this move was possibly orchestrated by ser <ALLISER THORNE> to punish <JON SNOW> , it is also an opportunity for the lord commander to groom <JON SNOW> directly for command . both are then surprised when <PYPAR> admits that he was sent to the watch for refusing to give sexual favors to a lord , not for stealing a wheel of cheese to feed his sister as he had previously claimed . nothing about being sent to the wall is fair . . 
 <JON SNOW> and <SAMWELL TARLY> swear their oaths to the night's watch . 
convinced , <JON SNOW> , along with <SAM> , say their oath of fealty to the night's watch in front of a heart tree just inside the eaves of the haunted <FOREST> and are acknowledged as <TOMMEN> of the watch . <SAM> decided to take the oath with <JON SNOW> to the old gods of the <FOREST> , as the <SEVEN KINGDOMS> gods his father worshiped have never seemed to answer him . after they take their oaths , ghost finds a severed <HAND> in the woods and brings it back to <JON SNOW> and a horrified <SAM> . 
 <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> tries to convince <KHAL DROGO> to invade <WESTEROS> . 
the wine seller is captured after trying to poison <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> . in <VAES DOTHRAK> , <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> attempts to convince <KHAL DROGO> about the benefits of an invasion of the <SEVEN KINGDOMS> , but <KHAL DROGO> is reluctant to cross the <NARROW SEA> , despite the thousands of ships they could find in the <FREE CITIES> to do the job . he says that a woman doesn't need an iron chair but only a horse . <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> travels to the marketplace with ser <JORAH MORMONT> and her handmaidens . she asks <JORAH MORMONT> to help convince her husband since the <SEVEN KINGDOMS> are hers by birthright but he reminds her that her ancestor <AEGON> the conqueror took six of the <SEVEN KINGDOMS> , because he was capable of doing so due to his dragons , nothing more . <JORAH MORMONT> is delivered a message from <VARYS> , a royal pardon for his crimes he quickly realizes that this news would only come if he was no longer needed as a spy . seeing <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> with a wineseller who is keen for her to try a particular vintage from the arbor , <JORAH MORMONT> realizes that the wine has been poisoned this is the assassination attempt . having second thoughts , he steps in and stops <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> from drinking it . the wineseller attempts to flee , but <RAKHARO> brings him down with a bolo tangling his ankles . 
with the wine seller captured , ser <JORAH MORMONT> tells <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> that <ROBERT BARATHEON> will never stop trying to kill her and her future children . <KHAL DROGO> quickly arrives in the tent . he glares at the seller and then goes to <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> to ensure she is okay , before offering <JORAH MORMONT> the reward of any horse he chooses for foiling the assassination . angered , he begins to yell out in dothraki that his <ARMY> will cross the poison water as no khalasar has done before and take the <IRON THRONE> for his son . <KHAL DROGO>'s khalasar departs <VAES DOTHRAK> the next morning , with the wine seller tied naked to the saddle of <DAENERYS TARGARYEN>' horse , forced to walk until he eventually falls of exhaustion and is dragged to his death . 
lord <EDDARD STARK> meets with <CERSEI LANNISTER> . he tells her that he knows the secret that <JON ARRYN> died for that <CERSEI LANNISTER>'s three children are not <ROBERT BARATHEON>'s , but the product of incest between her and <JAIME LANNISTER> . <CERSEI LANNISTER> does not deny the charge and in fact is proud of it , comparing their love to the old <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> practice of marrying brother to sister she also admits to having despised <ROBERT BARATHEON> ever since their wedding night , when <ROBERT BARATHEON> drunkenly stumbled into <CERSEI LANNISTER>'s bed and called her lyanna . <EDDARD STARK> angrily tells her to take her children and leave the city immediately . when <ROBERT BARATHEON> returns from his hunt , he will tell him the truth of the matter and <CERSEI LANNISTER> should run as far as she can before that happens , lest <ROBERT BARATHEON>'s wrath find her . 
 <CERSEI LANNISTER> icily calls ned a fool for turning down the <IRON THRONE> himself after the <SACK> of king's <LANDING> . <EDDARD STARK> tells her that he has regrets , but that isn't one of them . <CERSEI LANNISTER> departs with a chilling warning when you play the game of thrones , you <LUWIN> or you die . there is no middle ground . 
in one of his brothels , <LITTLEFINGER> instructs the newly arrived ros and another prostitute , armeca , on how to please their customers and make them happy . when they ask him to join them , he refuses , saying that he only ever had eyes for one woman . he tells them about his past , how he loved and fought a duel for a woman . he lost and subsequently realized that he could never beat those in power by honorable means , as they would never let him compete on equal terms . when ros asks him what he wants , he says , oh , everything . . 
 <ROBERT BARATHEON> signs a document confirming <EDDARD STARK> as <PROTECTOR> of the <REALM> . <RENLY> finds <EDDARD STARK> and tells him that <ROBERT BARATHEON> has been badly mauled by a boar and is not expected to survive . <EDDARD STARK> finds <ROBERT BARATHEON> telling joffrey that he wishes he could have been a better father to him . <EDDARD STARK> chooses not to tell <ROBERT BARATHEON> about his discoveries to spare his final hours from pain . <ROBERT BARATHEON> instructs <EDDARD STARK> to take a letter naming him as the lord <PROTECTOR> of the <REALM> , to rule until joffrey comes of age . <EDDARD STARK> does not write joffrey's name , instead saying the rightful heir . <ROBERT BARATHEON> also asks him to cancel the attempt on <DAENERYS TARGARYEN>'s life . leaving the chamber , <EDDARD STARK> talks to <VARYS> , who slyly points out that <LANCEL LANNISTER> ensured the king kept refreshed with alcohol during the hunt , meaning his reactions were slowed and unreliable . <VARYS> also says it is far too late to stop the attempt on <DAENERYS TARGARYEN>' life . 
the letter ned sends to <STANNIS BARATHEON> , informing him of his findings . 
at king's <LANDING> , <RENLY> confronts <EDDARD STARK> and offers him a hundred swords to take the queen and her children into custody , but <EDDARD STARK> refuses to dishonor <ROBERT BARATHEON>'s last hours by shedding blood in the <RED KEEP> and taking frightened children hostage . <RENLY> suggests that he could make a good king , but <EDDARD STARK> angrily points out that <STANNIS BARATHEON> is <RENLY>'s older brother and the true heir . in his study he writes a letter laying out his findings to lord <STANNIS BARATHEON> and instructs a courier to take the message to <DRAGONSTONE> , <STANNIS BARATHEON>'s island fortress . <LITTLEFINGER> then arrives and talks to <EDDARD STARK> , who tells him the truth about joffrey's parentage . <LITTLEFINGER> suggests that they <RED KEEP> quiet , acknowledge joffrey as king and make him their puppet . if he proves intractable , they can reveal the truth and crown the more malleable <RENLY> instead . <EDDARD STARK> considers this treason . <LITTLEFINGER> realizes that even though lord <EDDARD STARK> has <ROBERT BARATHEON>'s edict naming him regent and <PROTECTOR> of the <REALM> , he doesn't have the <TOMMEN> he needs to seize control from <CERSEI LANNISTER> . he needs the loyalty of the <CITY WATCH> . <LITTLEFINGER> understands that the honorable <EDDARD STARK> can't come right out and ask him to bribe them , but agrees to do what needs to be done . 
 <EDDARD STARK> confronts king joffrey in the <IRON THRONE> room . 
in king's <LANDING> , <EDDARD STARK> is summoned to the <IRON THRONE> room by king joffrey <ROBERT BARATHEON> has died . he arrives to find <LITTLEFINGER> and <VARYS> waiting for him , along with commander <JANOS SLYNT> and a detachment of the <CITY WATCH> . <VARYS> tells him that <RENLY> has fled the <CITY WATCH> , along with ser <LORAS> tyrell and a number of retainers . they were last seen heading <SOUTH> . the party enters the <IRON THRONE> room , where joffrey sits on the <IRON THRONE> . he demands oaths of fealty from his councilors and subjects . instead , <EDDARD STARK> gives ser <BARRISTAN SELMY> the proclamation naming him as lord <PROTECTOR> of the <REALM> . to <BARRISTAN SELMY>'s shock , <CERSEI LANNISTER> takes the paper shield and tears it up . instead , she suggests that <EDDARD STARK> bend the knee and swear allegiance . in return he will be allowed to return to winterfell . <EDDARD STARK> responds that joffrey has no claim to the <IRON THRONE> and commands <JANOS SLYNT> to take the queen and her son into custody . instead , the <CITY WATCH> kill <EDDARD STARK>'s bodyguards and <LITTLEFINGER> holds a knife to his throat , saying , i did warn you not to trust me . 
you <LUWIN> or you die is the seventh episode of the first season of game of thrones . it is the seventh episode of the series overall . it first aired on 29 may 2011 , but some hbo subscribers were able to see it a week early on the hbo go digital platform . it was written by executive producers david benioff d.b . <WEISS> and directed by daniel minahan . 
the <CERSEI LANNISTER> <ARMY> , poised to invade the <RIVERLANDS> . 

 <JON ARRYN> and <SAM> return to <CASTLE BLACK> with their party and two dead bodies in tow . the two corpses are identified as members of <BENJEN> <EDDARD STARK>'s missing ranging party , jafer flowers and othor . though the deceased appear to have been dead for some time , <SAM> astutely notes that the bodies do not smell like they have been rotting . <JON ARRYN> and several other sworn <BROTHERS> urge lord commander <JEOR MORMONT> to burn the bodies , but he refuses , wanting maester <AEMON> to examine them . 
 <JON ARRYN> is summoned to <JEOR MORMONT>'s chambers as news has arrived of <EDDARD STARK>'s arrest and imprisonment . after being given the letter to read for himself , a speechless <JON ARRYN> attempts to leave before <JEOR MORMONT> reminds him of the oath he has sworn to the night's <CITY WATCH> . when <JON ARRYN> expresses concern for his sisters , <JEOR MORMONT> replies he is sure they are unharmed , though <JON ARRYN> is doubtful . 
later on , <ALLISER THORNE> taunts <JON ARRYN> that his father is a traitor , calling him , not just a bastard , a traitor's bastard . <JON ARRYN> angrily charges at him with a knife and <ALLISER THORNE> is only saved by <GRENN> and <PYP> holding <JON ARRYN> back . commander <JEOR MORMONT> witnessed the incident and confines <JON ARRYN> to quarters for his trouble . that night , <JON ARRYN> is aroused by a whining ghost scratching at the door . sensing trouble , <JON ARRYN> and his direwolf head to the lord commander's chambers where <JON ARRYN> is confronted by a wight , the reanimated corpse of the dead night's watchman . though <JON ARRYN> is able to stab the wight through the chest with his sword , the wight simply removes the sword and is unharmed . <JEOR MORMONT> appears , seeking out the commotion . <JON ARRYN> grabs <JEOR MORMONT>'s oil lamp and throws it at the wight , finally destroying it . 
the morning after , the two wight bodies have been thoroughly burned . <SAM> says he read in a book that the dead are animated by the touch of the <WHITE WALKERS> and only fire can destroy such creatures . he hopes the wall is big enough to <HOLD> them back when the <WHITE WALKERS> come in force . 
at the <EYRIE> , catelyn is furious with lysa first for lysa not immediately notifying her about <EDDARD STARK>'s arrest and second for refusing to consider summoning the knights of the <VALE> to war . despite setting in motion this chain of events with her letter to her sister regarding the murder of <JON ARRYN> , lysa does not believe that war is in the <VALE>'s best interests and rather want the knights to stay in the <VALE> to protect her son and their lord . 
tyrion and bronn have reached the western edge of the <VALE> and are surrounded by members of the hill tribes , led by a fearsome warrior named <SHAGGA> . at first he orders them to be killed , but tyrion does some fast talking and convinces the hill tribes that <HOUSE LANNISTER> is an enemy of the <HOUSE ARRYN> and its rulers . he proposes an alliance which will allow the tribes to enact vengeance against <HOUSE ARRYN> and take ownership of the <RIVERLANDS> of the <VALE> . they eagerly agree , and escort tyrion and bronn westwards towards where the <HOUSE LANNISTER> armies are gathering . 
dozens of ravens leaving winterfell , summoning the banners of the north to war . 
robb receives a letter from sansa in king's <LANDING> , asking him to pledge fealty to king joffrey . maester <LUWIN> correctly deduces the letter is actually the work of the queen . robb refuses to consider the request and sends out ravens , summoning the lords bannermen of the north and their armies to assemble at winterfell . released ravens fill the sky . 
at winterfell , robb holds a feast for several of his newly arrived bannermen . <JON ARRYN> umber assumes that he will lead the vanguard , and is offended by the suggestion that he would be made to march behind a glover , threatening to withdraw from the host . in response , robb promises that , after the conflict with the <LANNISTERS> , he will oust <GREATJON> from his <RED KEEP> and hang him for breaking his oaths to <HOUSE STARK> when the enraged bannerman goes to draw a weapon , robb's direwolf <GREY WIND> sets upon him , biting off two of his <FINGERS> . robb recites'that it is death to bear steel against your liege lord' but then diffuses the situation by excusing <GREATJON>'s aggression , saying that'doubtless , the <GREATJON> only meant to cut my meat for me' . the <GREATJON> roars with laughter and accepts robb's commands , much to the shock of bran , who witnessed the entire incident . robb says farewell to bran and to <RICKON> , who is convinced he'll see neither robb nor his parents again . 
bran prays by the heart tree when he is approached by <OSHA> who tells him the <HOLD> gods of the <FOREST> are listening to him and that the <WILDLINGS> also worship the <HOLD> gods . she laments that the <SOUTH> has lost touch with the past the southern weirwoods were cut down years ago and the southerners have no idea what's awakening in the north . they are interrupted by <HODOR> who was bathing and has forgotten to put his clothes back on , and <OSHA> remarks that he might have giant blood in him before bran sends him away . curious , bran asks her if giants live <BEYOND> the wall . she affirms they do , as well has many other beings , though not all of them are friendly . she asserts that the <ARMY> robb has gathered should be marching north , not <SOUTH> . 
catelyn and ser <RODRIK CASSEL> intercept robb's <ARMY> in the <NECK> as it presses southwards . robb initially exclaims with excitement upon seeing his mother , but stops short of embracing her lest he look weak in front of his bannermen . catelyn looks at her son with understanding , later embracing once their liege lords have left their tent . she tells robb he has no choice but to go to war . however , he can not lose , for the sake of ned , sansa , and arya , as if he is defeated , <TYWIN LANNISTER> will show their family no mercy . 
later on , robb and his lords are debating on the route of their march , and on whether to march directly against <TYWIN LANNISTER>'s <ARMY> or against jaime's <ARMY> besieging <RIVERRUN> . to get to jaime , they need to cross the green fork of the river <TRIDENT> , and the only crossing is at the <TWINS> , held by the notoriously prickly and easily offended lord <WALDER FREY> . a <TYWIN LANNISTER> scout is captured , and robb sends him back to warn lord <TYWIN LANNISTER> that twenty thousand <NORTHERN> soldiers are marching against him . 
 <KEVAN> and <TYWIN LANNISTER> greet tyrion and his companions . tyrion , bronn , <SHAGGA> and the rest of the hill tribesmen arrive at the <TYWIN LANNISTER> encampment , to find lord <TYWIN LANNISTER> and his brother , ser <KEVAN> , planning to engage the <HOUSE STARK> <ARMY> , which is moving <SOUTH> from the <NECK> . <TYWIN LANNISTER> shows no sign of relief that his son is alive . <TYWIN LANNISTER> accepts the aid of the hill tribesmen , but <SHAGGA> will only fight if tyrion fights alongside them , a prospect which <TYWIN LANNISTER> welcomes and terrifies tyrion . 
 <KHAL DROGO> disciplines <MAGO> . daenerys notes <KHAL DROGO>'s injury . in essos , <KHAL DROGO> having taken an oath to take the <IRON THRONE> , has begun his march of conquest to the <NARROW SEA> . the dothraki raid a village in lhazar , a peaceful country to the <SOUTH> east of <VAES DOTHRAK> . to finance the war to come , they must raid villages and take people to sell into slavery , thereby gaining the money to hire ships for the khalasar to assault <WESTEROS> . ser jorah and others try to explain this to daenerys , but she is disturbed to see the aftermath , the dothraki killing the villagers and raping their women , and orders it stopped . the dothraki grow angry at not being able to take the spoils of victory , as that is the dothraki way . she starts claiming all the women they see to protect them . the angry warriors take their complaints to <KHAL DROGO> , but he is amused at his wife's fierceness . he tells them that daenerys may <RED KEEP> the women she has claimed , they can find others . one man won't listen , and angrily accuses <KHAL DROGO> of being slave to a foreign whore . <KHAL DROGO> stops the complaints by killing <MAGO> , the offended warrior who challenges him . <KHAL DROGO> takes a deep wound to the chest in the process . though <KHAL DROGO> dismisses it as a scratch , daenerys insists it be treated and allows one of the women she rescued , a healer called mirri maz duur to treat the wound , despite the distaste of <KHAL DROGO>'s bloodriders , who derisively call the woman maegi a witch . 
 <TYWIN LANNISTER> soldiers complete their purge of the <HOUSE STARK> guards and household staff . sansa and <SEPTA MORDANE> hear sounds of fighting . when they are confronted by <TYWIN LANNISTER> guardsmen led by <SANDOR CLEGANE> , <SEPTA MORDANE> tells sansa to run and lock herself in her room while she stays to confront them . however , <SANDOR CLEGANE> later finds and takes sansa into custody . . 
 <SYRIO FOREL> confronts ser <MERYN TRANT> and <TYWIN LANNISTER> guards . 
more <TYWIN LANNISTER> guardsmen , this time led by ser <MERYN TRANT> of the <KINGSGUARD> , interrupt a dancing lesson between <SYRIO FOREL> and arya . <SYRIO FOREL> holds arya back , questioning why lord eddard would send <TYWIN LANNISTER> men to find arya . she then refuses to go with them , and when they try to force the issue <SYRIO FOREL> disarms and disables all of the lightly armored guardsmen with his wooden practice sword . he tells arya to run as he faces down <MERYN TRANT> , noting that for himself , the first sword of <BRAAVOS> does not run . <SYRIO FOREL>'s fate after this is unclear . 
arya runs to the stables where the men waiting with their baggage were supposed to be to take them to the ship for winterfell . the men are dead , but she finds her real sword , <NEEDLE> , in the bottom of her trunk . arya then starts to leave the stables . arya knows how to get out of the <RED KEEP> via the tunnel under the castle that she found when she was chasing cats and followed the two conspirators . when a stableboy tries to grab her , arya turns around brandishing <NEEDLE> and accidentally runs him through and kills him . horrified , she flees . 
 <VARYS> visits <EDDARD STARK> in his cell in the dungeons . he is incredulous that <EDDARD STARK> trusted <LITTLEFINGER> over him , and even more so that he warned cersei what he was going to do . <EDDARD STARK> says he wanted to extend mercy to cersei's children , whom robert would have killed if he'd known the truth . <VARYS> bluntly tells <EDDARD STARK> that his mercy is what killed king robert , to <EDDARD STARK>'s shame . <VARYS> then tells him that catelyn also no longer holds tyrion as her prisoner , meaning that the <STARKS> have nothing to barter with for <EDDARD STARK>'s life . when <EDDARD STARK> suggests they should just kill him , <VARYS> says not today , my lord . as he departs , <EDDARD STARK> asks <VARYS> who he truly serves <VARYS> , in a rare display of honesty , replies the <REALM> , my lord . someone must . 
cersei and the remainder of the <SMALL COUNCIL> , comprised of <GRAND> maester <PYCELLE> , <VARYS> , and <LITTLEFINGER> , summon sansa to inform her that her father has been arrested for treason . they manipulate sansa into writing a letter to her brother robb , asking him to bend the knee peacefully to joffrey . they add that <EDDARD STARK>'s fate may depend on what his son and the other <NORTHERN> lords do . sansa agrees to write the letter . 
later on , king joffrey holds court in the <RED KEEP> . <JANOS SLYNT> , commander of the <CITY WATCH> , is to be made lord of harrenhal as a reward for his loyal service . cersei then dismisses ser <BARRISTAN SELMY> as head of the <KINGSGUARD> , noting that the time has come for an honorable retirement . <BARRISTAN SELMY> is confused , pointing out that <KINGSGUARD> serve for life , but joffrey angrily says that <BARRISTAN SELMY> is too old , and couldn't protect his father . <BARRISTAN SELMY>'s disgrace is only compounded when he learns his post as lord commander is to be given to <JAIME LANNISTER> , much to his disgust . <VARYS> announces that <BARRISTAN SELMY> is to be given a castle and land in recognition of his years of service , but the old knight , insulted by what he sees as being offered a hall to die in and men to bury me , takes off his armor , throws his sword at joffrey's feet and storms out , stating that he could still kill all five of the other <KINGSGUARD> present with ease . 
sansa begs joffrey for her father's life , claiming that the medicine he was taking for his injured leg was responsible for his treasonous talk . joffrey says that her sweet words have moved him and he will spare <EDDARD STARK> , if he bends the knee to him and acknowledges him as king . sansa says he will . 
the pointy end is the eighth episode of the first season of game of thrones . it is the eighth episode of the series overall . it first aired on june 5 , 2011. it was written by executive producer george r.r . martin and directed by daniel minahan . 
in the aftermath of ned s capture , <SYRIO FOREL> and arya face off against <JAIME LANNISTER> guards , while cersei manipulates sansa to her own ends . robb rallies his father s <NORTHERN> bannermen against <TYWIN LANNISTER> and heads <SOUTH> to war . tyrion forms an uneasy alliance with the hill tribes and reunites with his father . jon lashes out at ser <ALLISER THORNE> and battles a mysterious attacker from <BEYOND> the wall . <DANY> is forced to reconcile her desire to <CONQUER> <WESTEROS> with <KHAL DROGO> s savagery after the dothraki raid a peaceful village . 

theon and robb <OUTSIDE> the <TWINS> . robb's <ARMY> has reached the <TWINS> , the heavily fortified crossing over the green fork of <TRIDENT> river . <THEON GREYJOY> shoots down messenger ravens , so no word of their presence can be relayed , but finds nothing more but messages to extended family members . to enter the castle would be perilous for robb , so <CATELYN STARK> enters to negotiate their crossing the river . 
though held by <HOUSE FREY> , bannermen to <CATELYN STARK>'s father , lord <WALDER FREY> has not yet taken up arms . when called up , he says he had been preparing to march , and was just waiting for all his forces to arrive . in reality , he waited to see which side was winning before deciding whether to get involved . now , as the tully's <ARMY> has been defeated and <RIVERRUN> is held by the <LANNISTERS> , he wants to know why he should be helping robb and taking up arms against the king . after some hard bargaining between <CATELYN STARK> and <WALDER FREY> , they strike a deal the <FREYS> will join robb's cause , allow him to cross and commit troops to his <ARMY> , but in return both robb and arya must each marry one of <WALDER FREY>'s own children . robb agrees , though noting that arya won't like it . robb must also take <OLYVAR> <WALDER FREY> as a squire . 
the <TYWIN LANNISTER> armies prepare for <BATTLE> . <TYWIN LANNISTER> tells his son tyrion that he means to use the hill tribe forces to give them an edge against the <CATELYN STARK> <ARMY> , essentially to be used as cannon fodder . he orders tyrion to lead them from the front of the vanguard . tyrion angrily accuses his father of trying to kill him . he storms back to his tent to find that bronn has found him , as per instruction , a whore named <SHAE> . tyrion takes an immediate liking to her . when told they go into <BATTLE> in the vanguard in the morning , bronn goes off to find one for himself . 
tyrion , bronn , and <SHAE> play a drinking game the knight before the <BATTLE> . tyrion makes observations and if he is correct the person has to drink . he guesses correctly that bronn has been <BEYOND> the wall and killed someone before he was twelve years old though it was a woman , not a woman , and he killed her in self defense , because she was coming at him with an axe . tyrion guesses that <SHAE>'s mother was a whore , her father deserted them , and she is low born however he is wrong on each guess . tyrion can not read <SHAE>'s personality , but this only makes her more intriguing to him . when <SHAE> starts to question tyrion , bronn reveals that he heard tyrion was once married . reluctantly , tyrion explains that when he was very young , he and <JAIME LANNISTER> were out riding near <CASTERLY ROCK> and found a young common girl in distress from bandits . while <JAIME LANNISTER> chased the bandits off , tyrion comforted the girl , whose name was tysha . they ended up getting drunk at a local inn , and she became so enamored of him that tyrion felt like he wasn't an ugly dwarf . later that knight she had sex with tyrion , the first time he was ever with a woman . tyrion fell madly in love , and bribed a drunken septon to marry them in secret . . 
however , two weeks later his father <TYWIN LANNISTER> found out , and was utterly furious that his son had married a commoner . <TYWIN LANNISTER> forced <JAIME LANNISTER> to reveal the truth the girl was a prostitute and <JAIME LANNISTER> set the situation up to do something nice for his little brother . <TYWIN LANNISTER> then instructed his guards to have sex with her , with her being paid a silver coin for each woman , while tyrion was forced to <CITY WATCH> . <SHAE> points out that tyrion was foolish to believe a woman would sleep with him just hours after almost being raped . as she gets romantic with tyrion , bronn leaves the tent . <TYRION LANNISTER> leads the hill tribes into <BATTLE> . the next morning the <TYRION LANNISTER> <ARMY> finds that the <STARKS> have stolen a march on them they are about to be attacked and have to hastily prepare for <BATTLE> . <TYRION LANNISTER> gives a rousing speech to his hill tribesmen , but as they charge for the front he is first nearly trampled and then knocked out by an accidental blow to the head from someone's club . when he regains consciousness on the back of a wagon , bronn tells him that the <LANNISTERS> won the <BATTLE> , but it was a feint . as a diversion , robb sent a small portion of his <ARMY> to confront and delay <TYWIN LANNISTER>'s forces , while the main <ARMY> marched on <RIVERRUN> to attack <JAIME LANNISTER>'s <ARMY> . <JAIME LANNISTER> is captured by robb's <ARMY> . <ROBB STARK> after his victory . 
 <CATELYN STARK> and ser <RODRIK CASSEL> are waiting in woodlands as they hear sounds of <BATTLE> . suddenly <ROBB STARK> returns from his victory with his guards and a prisoner , <JAIME LANNISTER> himself . the <BATTLE> of the <WHISPERING WOOD> has lifted the <SIEGE> of <RIVERRUN> , and <JAIME LANNISTER>'s <ARMY> has been destroyed . <JAIME LANNISTER> suggests they end the war now with a bout of single combat between himself and <ROBB STARK> , but <ROBB STARK> refuses and has him imprisoned . <ROBB STARK> laments that his diversion sent 2 , 000 men to their deaths . he gives a speech to his <ARMY> and tells them that they have won a great victory , but the war is far from over . 
 <JEOR MORMONT> gives his sword <LONGCLAW> to <JON SNOW> . at <CASTLE BLACK> , lord commander <JEOR MORMONT> gives <JON SNOW> a <VALYRIAN> steel sword , <LONGCLAW> , in thanks for saving his life . <JEOR MORMONT> also reinstates <JON SNOW> to his former position and tells him he has dispatched ser <ALLISER THORNE> to king's <LANDING> to lay the <HAND> of the wight they found at the feet of the king and ask for aid . 
maester <AEMON> reveals his true identity . 
 <JEOR MORMONT> explains to <JON SNOW> that <LONGCLAW> was meant for his own son , ser <JORAH MORMONT> , but he disgraced himself and fled in exile to essos . <JON SNOW> goes to the dining hall and the other recruits make a fuss over the sword , but <SAMWELL TARLY> seems distant from the revelry . <SAM> takes <JON SNOW> aside and informs him about <ROBB STARK> leading an <ARMY> <SOUTH> to war . <JON SNOW> ponders that he should be with him , but maester <AEMON> tells him their duty to the knight's <CITY WATCH> comes first . to <JON SNOW>'s surprise , <AEMON> reveals that his full name is <AEMON> targaryen , the son of a king , brother to another , the uncle of the <MAD> king . <AEMON> had to stand aside and do nothing while his entire family was butchered or exiled during robert's <REBELLION> . it is not an easy life they have chosen . <AEMON> remarks that he can not make <JON SNOW> stay or go like the maester , <JON SNOW> must make the choice himself , and live with the consequences of it for the rest of his life . 
drogo after his fall . far to the east , <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> is concerned that the wound her husband <KHAL DROGO> took fighting <MAGO> has festered and become infected . he falls from his horse , a grave sign of weakness amongst the dothraki . <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> tells the khalasar that they are stopping and requests for <QOTHO> to get mirri maz duur to help <KHAL DROGO> . <QOTHO> is unhappy with entrusting <KHAL DROGO>'s care to the woman , whom he calls a maegi or witch , but relents . 
at <DAENERYS TARGARYEN>' request , ser <JORAH MORMONT> armors himself . <JORAH MORMONT> also advises her to leave now , because <KHAL DROGO> is certain to die and when he dies , his lieutenants will fight amongst themselves to be his successor whoever wins will kill <DAENERYS TARGARYEN>'s son , rather than risk the boy growing up to be a rival , but <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> refuses to abandon her husband . mirri maz duur promises to save <KHAL DROGO>'s life , but she needs to sacrifice a life in exchange . she takes <KHAL DROGO>'s horse into his tent and starts the ceremony , slitting the animal's throat over <KHAL DROGO>'s comatose form . . 
 <JORAH MORMONT> helps <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> . 
some of <KHAL DROGO>'s warriors become enraged at what they see as <DAENERYS TARGARYEN>' attempts to interfere with the natural way of things and <QOTHO> tries to attack her , but ser <JORAH MORMONT> kills him . <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> starts to go into labor , but none of the dothraki midwives will help her , thinking she is cursed . with no choice , <JORAH MORMONT> takes <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> into the tent as the ceremony continues . 
 <VARYS> visits <EDDARD STARK> in the dungeons under the <RED KEEP> . <VARYS> tells <EDDARD STARK> that sansa begged for his life before the whole court and that <ROBB STARK> is leading an <ARMY> from the north . in addition , the queen is more concerned over the intentions of king robert's brother , stannis , a proven <BATTLE> commander known to be without mercy . for the sake of sansa's life , <VARYS> urges <EDDARD STARK> to confess to treason . in return , cersei will let him take the <CASTLE BLACK> and join his younger brother <BENJEN> and bastard son <JON SNOW> on the wall . <EDDARD STARK> is angered by the suggestion that he would trade in his honesty and honor for his life , though he appears to have second thoughts when <VARYS> insinuates that sansa would pay the price for his defiance . 
 <ARYA STARK> is living rough on the streets of the <CITY WATCH> . she catches a pigeon and tries to trade it for a slice of bread , to no avail . she sees crowds moving through the streets and is told that the <HAND> of the king is being brought before the great sept of baelor , the center of religious worship in the <CITY WATCH> . stunned that she will see her father she drops the pigeon and joins the crowd . unable to see , she climbs unto the pedestal of a statue of baelor a previous <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> king , baelor the blessed , for whom the sept is named . she sees her father being brought in chains to the steps of the temple . he sees <ARYA STARK> on the statue , and as he is dragged through the crowd he passes <YOREN> of the knight's <CITY WATCH> who had met <ARYA STARK> . lord <EDDARD STARK> looks at the statue and says , baelor , puzzling the crowd . <YOREN> understands , however , and moves toward the statue where <ARYA STARK> is watching . 
 <EDDARD STARK> is given a chance to confess his crimes . he weighs his choices as he sees both <ARYA STARK> and sansa present , and chooses to save them by making a false confession . he says that joffrey is the true king on the <IRON THRONE> , pleasing him . <GRAND> maester <PYCELLE> extols the virtues of mercy and joffrey agrees that he could be merciful and send <EDDARD STARK> to the knight's <CITY WATCH> as his mother has suggested and as sansa has begged . he instead acknowledges that as women they are soft and treason must never go unpunished . he commands ser <ILYN PAYNE> to bring him the traitor's head . . 
ser <ILYN PAYNE> executes <EDDARD STARK> . 
the crowd goes into an uproar . <ARYA STARK> tries to make her way through the crowd drawing her sword to save her father , but <YOREN> grabs and stops her , shielding her from seeing her father's death . sansa screams and is restrained by guards . a visibly horrified cersei frantically tries to persuade her son to reconsider , as does <VARYS> , but there is no time . forced to kneel , <EDDARD STARK> looks at the statue and sees that <ARYA STARK> has been rescued by <YOREN> , and is relieved that she is safe . ser <ILYN PAYNE> draws <EDDARD STARK>'s own sword , <ICE> , and cuts his head off with a single blow . a flock of pigeons takes flight immediately afterwards , the <SIGHT> being all <ARYA STARK> needs to know her father is dead . 
baelor is the ninth episode of the first season of game of thrones . it is the ninth episode of the series overall . it first aired on june 12 , 2011. it was written by executive producers david benioff d.b . <WEISS> and directed by alan taylor . 
with sansa s life in danger , ned makes a fateful decision . catelyn brokers an unsavory deal with the slippery <WALDER FREY> . tyrion acquires a mistress and is forced by his father to fight on the front lines . <ROBB STARK> wins his first major victory and captures a prized prisoner . <JON SNOW> is rewarded for his valor and discovers a dark secret about maester <AEMON> . as <KHAL DROGO> s wound festers , <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> defies his bloodrider <QOTHO> and puts her trust in the enslaved witch mirri maz duur . 

at the great sept of baelor , <EDDARD STARK> has been executed by beheading the great sword <ICE> is covered in blood , and <SANDOR CLEGANE> standing next to ser <ILYN PAYNE> , the royal executioner , holds lord <EDDARD STARK>'s head up to the adulation of the baying crowd . <SANSA STARK> has fainted . in the crowd , <YOREN> drags <ARYA STARK> away , making a point of calling her boy . once he gets her out of the courtyard , he cuts her hair off with a knife . he tells her that he will get her out of king's <LANDING> and to winterfell as a recruit of the knight's <CITY WATCH> , but he warns her not to trust the other recruits , since apparently half would <HAND> her over to cersei for a pardon , while the other half would do the same , but only after raping her first . 
joffrey is holding court and a singer is brought before him , charged with making up an amusing but offensive song about robert and cersei . the song says that the boar might have killed king robert , but the <REBELLION> in his bed had previously castrated him . the singer turns out to be <MARILLION> , who catelyn and ser rodrik met at the inn at the crossroads , and who accompanied them and tyrion to the <VALE> of arryn . joffrey asks <MARILLION> if he wants to <RED KEEP> his hands or tongue . <MARILLION> fearfully responds that everyone needs hands . joffrey commands <ILYN PAYNE> to cut out the tongue instead . joffrey then takes <SANSA STARK> up to the walls to see her father's head and makes her look at it . he cruelly mocks her , promising he will give her <ROBB STARK>'s head next . <SANSA STARK> quietly retorts that <ROBB STARK> might give her joffrey's instead . infuriated , joffrey orders ser <MERYN TRANT> to beat her , as cersei has told him that a king should not hit his queen . <SANSA STARK> moves up behind joffrey , apparently preparing to shove him off the walkway to his death , but unexpectedly <SANDOR CLEGANE> dabs the blood off her lip with a handkerchief and after joffrey leaves , tells her to give him what he wants . 
lancel and cersei . 
 <CERSEI LANNISTER> has taken a new lover , her cousin lancel who was king robert's squire . she also receives a letter informing her of jaime's capture . lancel is naked in <CERSEI LANNISTER>'s bedroom . the thought of being at war is exciting to him , as he has just been made a new young knight . he asks for the news of the war and asks what their next move is , but <CERSEI LANNISTER> tells him to shut up and get back in bed . 
 <GRAND> maester <PYCELLE> takes the prostitute ros to bed , revealing that he is actually far less frail than he appears . he boasts to ros of the several great kings he has served , lamenting first how <AERYS TARGARYEN> devolved from a charming young man into a paranoid lunatic obsessed with fire , how <ROBERT BARATHEON> was a great soldier , but perhaps not so ideal a king , before displaying his sycophantic loyalty to joffrey . 
 <YOREN> and <ARYA STARK> . <YOREN> has assembled a band of new recruits for the knight's <CITY WATCH> . pretending that <ARYA STARK> is a boy called arry , he has her join the group . also in the group are <HOT PIE> , <LOMMY> greenhands , and <GENDRY> , who unknown to him , is king <ROBERT BARATHEON>'s bastard son . he had been working for tobho mott , but with <ROBERT BARATHEON> dead , the secret funds being sent to mott stopped , so he fired <GENDRY> and told him he had to join the knight's <CITY WATCH> . <HOT PIE> and <LOMMY> try to bully <ARYA STARK> into giving up <NEEDLE> , but she angrily draws the sword , warning that she has already killed one fat boy and will happily do it again . <GENDRY> breaks up the argument by taking <ARYA STARK>'s side , threatening the boys with violence to <RED KEEP> them from picking on <ARYA STARK> later . <YOREN> now has to get them all to the wall , a thousand leagues away , through the war torn <RIVERLANDS> . they set out . 
at winterfell , bran has another dream of the three eyed raven . he wakes up and tells <OSHA> about how the dream always ends with the bird flying into the crypts under the castle , and he tells her he thinks his father is in the tombs . <OSHA> takes bran down there , and bran tells her about the histories of some of the ancestors entombed there . they are then surprised by <SHAGGYDOG> , <RICKON>'s direwolf , who leaps out at them from the empty future tomb of <EDDARD STARK> . <RICKON> calls <SHAGGYDOG> off , then reveals to bran that he had the same dream . making their way out , <OSHA> is still trying to tell bran that it could be a coincidence , but <OUTSIDE> they see maester <LUWIN> , who holds a letter and looks at them with such sadness that it is obviously the news of <EDDARD STARK>'s death . 
catelyn comforts her son , promising to avenge <EDDARD STARK>'s death at <ROBB STARK>'s camp , catelyn stoically walks through the encampment and receives the condolences and respect of the <NORTHERN> bannermen , who bow to her as she passes . she makes her way into the woods around the camp . once she is out of everyone's <SIGHT> , she breaks down , practically hyperventilating with grief . hearing something from deeper in the woods , she finds <ROBB STARK> hacking his sword at a tree in anger and grief . lady catelyn calls to him and tells him he is ruining his sword . <ROBB STARK> drops the sword and falls into her arms , vowing to kill the <LANNISTERS> who murdered his father . catelyn comforts him and promises him revenge , but only after they rescue <SANSA STARK> and <ARYA STARK> first . 
at <ROBB STARK>'s camp , <ROBB STARK> and his bannermen debate what to do in the war against king joffrey . they debate whether to align with stannis or <RENLY> <ROBERT BARATHEON> , but there is no agreement as <RENLY> has greater forces , but stannis is elder and next in line of succession if <CERSEI LANNISTER>'s children are discounted . <JON SNOW> umber becomes irritated and questions why the <NORTHERNERS> should be told what to do by rulers in the <SOUTH> at all , reminding them that the north was once independent of the other kingdoms before the <TARGARYENS> threatened them with their dragons . with the dragons gone , umber declares there is only one king worthy of his respect and allegiance and bows before <ROBB STARK> , calling out , the king in the north the other <NORTHERN> bannermen take up the cry and bow before the new king in the north , swearing fealty to <ROBB STARK> . 
catelyn visits the captive <JAIME LANNISTER> who taunts her about ned's death and offers to serve her as a lover . she hits him in the head with a rock . <JAIME LANNISTER> says that if she keeps hitting him , she can kill him and that he doesn't fear death , though <JAIME LANNISTER> probably realizes that the <STARKS> won't kill him as long as his sister holds <SANSA STARK> and <ARYA STARK> hostage . catelyn tells him he has violated the laws of man and gods , and he asks where ned's gods were when his head was cut off he questions the existence of all gods , the old and the new . she says injustice in the world is because of men like him . <JAIME LANNISTER> responds , there are no men like me , only me . he admits to pushing bran from the tower , but doesn't reveal why . 
at the <JAIME LANNISTER> camp , lord tywin is holding a strategy meeting with his generals , and is furious that <JAIME LANNISTER> has been captured by the <STARKS> . both stannis and <RENLY> have claimed the <IRON THRONE> , meaning the <LANNISTERS> are now faced with fighting a two front war against the <STARKS> to the north and the <BARATHEONS> to the <SOUTH> . tywin's commanders are uncertain what to do , arguing about whether to strike while they still can , fall back and raise reinforcement armies , or sue for peace . tyrion points out that any chance of negotiating with <ROBB STARK> died when his father <EDDARD STARK> was executed . the <JAIME LANNISTER> <ARMY> is now exposed , so tywin decides to retreat to harrenhal , the great castle on the <NORTHERN> shores of gods eye , and use it as a base of operations . reluctantly impressed by tyrion's astute judgment of the situation , tywin orders his son to go to king's <LANDING> and serve as acting <HAND> of the king in tywin's stead . he is to bring <CERSEI LANNISTER> and joffrey to heel and prevent the young king from making more idiotic mistakes . tywin also tells him to deal with baelish , <VARYS> , and <PYCELLE> if he gets so much as a hint of treachery from any of them . he also orders tyrion to leave his whore behind . later on in his tent , tyrion complains about his father to <SHAE> , then decides to defy tywin and take <SHAE> to court anyway . 
 <JON SNOW> learns of his father's death . he saddles a horse and prepares to leave to join <ROBB STARK>'s <ARMY> , ignoring samwell's pleas to stay and fulfill his oaths . <JON SNOW> leaves <CASTLE BLACK> , but is pursued . one of his pursuers hits a tree branch and is unhorsed , and <JON SNOW> realizes it was <SAM> . he turns back to help him . the other riders are <GRENN> and <PYPAR> . he tells them to go back or they will get in trouble too , but they say they can't go back without him . they surround him and recite their oath to the knight's <CITY WATCH> , and <JON SNOW> realizes they are right leaving would make him a deserter and <OATHBREAKER> , something his father would never countenance if he were alive , and <JON SNOW> doesn't even know if <ROBB STARK> would accept his help or turn him over to the authorities . he agrees to return to the wall with them . 
lord commander <JEOR MORMONT> decides to overlook <JON SNOW>'s brief desertion , saying many have fled the wall , only to think better of it and return . if they executed everyone who did that , they'd have no men left . <JEOR MORMONT> tells <JON SNOW> that the war between the <LANNISTERS> and <STARKS> is less important than what they face now , a renewed threat from the <WILDLINGS> , <WHITE WALKERS> , and wights . <JEOR MORMONT> means to lead the knight's <CITY WATCH> in force into the haunted <FOREST> to learn more of their foe , to prepare to <BATTLE> against them , and to find the missing <BENJEN> <ROBB STARK> . <JON SNOW> agrees to commit himself fully to the knight's <CITY WATCH> and all that lies ahead . 
daenerys regains consciousness . in the wastelands <BEYOND> lhazar , daenerys wakes up to terrible news from ser <JORAH MORMONT> . her son , <RHAEGO> , is dead . he was born dead and deformed , covered with scales . the majority of the khalasar has also moved on , leaving them behind . however , drogo lives . daenerys insists on seeing her husband , and finds him a catatonic vegetable . daenerys demands to know why , and mirri maz duur explains that when daenerys saved her , she had already been raped three times and the temple she served had been burned and defiled by the dothraki . they had sacked her village , looted all they owned , and those not killed were enslaved . she has now gotten her revenge , not only on drogo , but on daenerys' child <RHAEGO> now her stallion who mounts the world can burn no cities and slaughter no innocents . duur agrees that daenerys saved her life , but she says to ask drogo what life is worth when all else is gone . 
it is knight , and daenerys is in their tent tending to drogo . she baths him , talks to him , even tries to seduce him , but nothing she does reaches him . she realizes he is no longer there , and seeing him in his vegetative state breaks her heart . crying , daenerys kisses him goodbye , then smothers him with a pillow . 
daenerys and her small retinue prepare a funeral pyre for drogo . she makes a speech to the few who are left saying that if they wish to go they may , but if they stay with her she will lead them into a glorious future . she frees those of them who are slaves and asks that they stay as equals . the maegi smirks as some people begin walking away . at daenerys' command , <RAKHARO> places the dragon eggs on the pyre , and mirri maz duur is tied to a stake next to the pyre as well . she tells daenerys that she will not scream while she is burned alive . daenerys replies that she only wants the maegi's life . ser <JORAH MORMONT> believes that daenerys intends to kill herself and pleads for her to reconsider , as they can sell the eggs and travel far away . ignoring <JORAH MORMONT>'s pleas , she kisses his cheek , and sets the pyre alight . mirri maz duur does indeed scream as she burns , and daenerys calmly walks into the flames . she stands below the pyre as flames appear to consume her . 
at dawn , the fire dies down . <JORAH MORMONT> and the rest of the khalasar awake to find daenerys sitting among the still smoldering embers , with three newly hatched baby dragons crawling over her . her clothes have burnt away and her body is covered in ash , but she is completely unharmed . one dragon nuzzles in her arm , another climbs her leg , and the third pulls itself up to sit on her shoulder . at the <SIGHT> of the mythical animals born anew , an amazed <JORAH MORMONT> and the few remaining dothraki kneel and swear their allegiance to the mother of dragons . after she slowly stands up from the ashes , the <CASTLE BLACK> hatchling on her shoulder rises , spreads its wings and screams , announcing the return of dragons to the world . 
fire and blood is the tenth and final episode of the first season of game of thrones . it is the tenth episode of the series overall . it first aired on june 19 , 2011. it was written by executive producers david benioff d.b . <WEISS> and directed by alan taylor .

sansa watches king joffrey's tournament . 
king <JOFFREY BARATHEON> holds a tournament to celebrate his nameday on the walls of the <RED KEEP> . he is irritated by ser <DONTOS> hollard , who arrives both late and intoxicated for his bout . <JOFFREY BARATHEON> orders his guards to pour an entire barrel of wine down <DONTOS>' throat with a funnel . <SANSA STARK> intercedes telling <JOFFREY BARATHEON> that ordering a death on one's name day is bad luck . <JOFFREY BARATHEON> dismisses this as a mindless superstition , but <SANDOR CLEGANE> seconds her . <SANSA STARK> convinces <JOFFREY BARATHEON> to instead make <DONTOS> his court fool , for which <DONTOS> is grateful . <TYRION LANNISTER> arrives back in king's <LANDING> , to <JOFFREY BARATHEON>'s disdain , but to the delight of <TOMMEN> and myrcella who had worried that he was dead . 
cersei is surprised to see <TYRION LANNISTER> return . 
the <SMALL COUNCIL> are in session to discuss the conclave's announcement that the long <SUMMER> has ended . cersei orders the <CITY WATCH> gates closed to refugees from the war in the <RIVERLANDS> . when <TYRION LANNISTER> arrives with a letter from lord tywin , appointing him as acting <HAND> of the king in tywin's stead , cersei becomes livid . she is suspicious that <TYRION LANNISTER> is taking power for himself , but he convinces her that he is there to act as an advisor . he criticizes his sister for failing to rein in <JOFFREY BARATHEON> and overseeing numerous bad decisions , particularly the execution of <NED STARK> . their actions have sparked a war , which , he adds , their side is currently losing . he is even more incredulous when he learns that <ARYA STARK> escaped , pointing out how much stronger their position could have been with three <ARYA STARK> hostages . <TYRION LANNISTER> hides his lover <SHAE> in his chambers in the tower of the <HAND> because he was forbidden by his father to bring her with him . she is initially thrilled at being brought to the capitol , and says that big cities make her want to <FUCK> . 
at winterfell , <BRAN STARK> suffers through the petty complaints of his vassals , facing unrest at <ROBB STARK> calling his banners and taking the young <TOMMEN> <SOUTH> . maester <LUWIN> guides him in carrying out a lord's duties . <BRAN STARK> dreams that he is his direwolf <SUMMER> walking in the godswood , and when he looks in the pool , he sees <SUMMER>'s reflection not his own which wakes him . he has <OSHA> and <HODOR> take him to the pool and is reassured to find that his waking reflection is his own . they discuss the phenomenon of the <RED COMET> , as many people think it means different things . <OSHA> tells him she believes it signifies the return of dragons to the world . 
stannis orders the burning of the seven to honor the lord of <LIGHT> . 
on the island of <DRAGONSTONE> , king <STANNIS BARATHEON> allows his advisor <MELISANDRE> to burn statues of the gods of the faith of the seven as an offering to her deity the lord of <LIGHT> . maester <CRESSEN> is outraged at the affront to his gods and fearful that <MELISANDRE> is leading <STANNIS BARATHEON> into a war that he can not <LUWIN> . <MELISANDRE> proclaims <STANNIS BARATHEON> a champion of the lord of <LIGHT> , as he draws a burning sword from one of the statues . <CRESSEN> asks <DAVOS> seaworth to help him intervene but <DAVOS> says that it is not the right time . 
 <STANNIS BARATHEON> dictates a letter about <JOFFREY BARATHEON>'s parentage . 
 <STANNIS BARATHEON> has received <NED STARK>'s letter , informing him that he was the true heir of king <ROBERT BARATHEON> , so he will send copies of a letter announcing his claim to the throne of the <SEVEN KINGDOMS> to lords throughout the <REALM> . he details the incestuous relationship between cersei and <JAIME LANNISTER> and challenges <JOFFREY BARATHEON>'s legitimacy . he rejects <DAVOS>'s appeal to consider an alliance with his brother <RENLY> <JOFFREY BARATHEON> , while <RENLY> is claiming the throne for himself , despite <RENLY> having widespread support , or even with <ROBB STARK> , since while <ROBB STARK> does not seek the <IRON THRONE> , he desires <NORTHERN> independence , which <STANNIS BARATHEON> sees as <ROBB STARK> stealing the <NORTHERN> half of his kingdom . <CRESSEN> feigns an apology in an effort to trick <MELISANDRE> into sharing a cup of poisoned wine with him . <DAVOS> sees him drop the poison in the cup , and tries to stop him . he drinks first and hands the cup to her . <MELISANDRE> is aware of what <CRESSEN> is doing , but smiling she drinks anyway and is unaffected by the poison , and <CRESSEN> dies in vain .

 <GREY WIND> and <JAIME LANNISTER> . 
 <ROBB STARK> receives the letter and interrogates the captive <JAIME LANNISTER> about his reasons for crippling <BRAN STARK> . <JAIME LANNISTER> reveals nothing and attacks <ROBB STARK>'s decision to <RED KEEP> him in his mobile camp rather than with one of his bannermen as demonstrating a lack of trust . <ROBB STARK> asserts his faith in his <TOMMEN> and his concern at the lengths <HOUSE LANNISTER> would go to in order to free <JAIME LANNISTER> . his direwolf <GREY WIND> is almost fully grown and menaces <JAIME LANNISTER> during the questioning . <ROBB STARK> sends his prisoner <ALTON LANNISTER> to king's <LANDING> with peace terms . his demands include the release of his sisters , the return of his father's remains along with the remains of all those who served him , and the recognition of the north as a free and independent kingdom . <THEON GREYJOY> appeals to <ROBB STARK> to send him to <PYKE> to seek an alliance with his father balon citing their need for a fleet in order to attack king's <LANDING> . catelyn counsels against putting trust in balon because of his history of <REBELLION> . she asks <ROBB STARK> to consider exchanging <JAIME LANNISTER> for his sisters . she then asks to return to her younger sons at winterfell but <ROBB STARK> tasks her with seeking an alliance with <RENLY> and sends ser <RODRIK CASSEL> instead to winterfell . 
cersei asks a favor of lord baelish . 
cersei tasks <PETYR> baelish with finding <ARYA STARK> . she needles <PETYR> about his unrequited love for catelyn and he counters by referencing her relationship with <JAIME LANNISTER> , telling her that knowledge is power . she responds by threatening his life in a demonstration of her control over her guards , ordering them to first seize baelish and cut his throat and almost immediately rescinding the order . she warns him that power is power . 
 <JOFFREY BARATHEON> redecorates his <IRON THRONE> room , hoping to restore the intimidating grandeur it held under the <TARGARYENS> . he refuses his mother's suggestion that they ask <TYWIN LANNISTER> for aid in the search for <ARYA STARK> because he does not feel it is necessary to find her and does not feel it is fitting for a king to ask for help . he blames <TYWIN LANNISTER> for their losses in the war and the capture of <JAIME LANNISTER> . having heard rumors about his parentage , he confronts his mother . she dismisses it as gossip spread by his enemies . he questions her about his father's bastard children and insults her by saying that <ROBERT BARATHEON> had grown tired of her . she slaps him , and he warns her never to hit him again under threat of death .

daenerys leads her people through the <RED WASTE> . 
 <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> leads her diminished khalasar east into the <RED WASTE> to avoid her rivals . she is surrounded by powerful enemies who ser jorah tells her will kill her and take her dragons . the deadly emptiness of the <RED WASTE> is her only option . she struggles to make her dragons eat what little meat she has , and her people face starvation . her beloved white mare , her first gift from <KHAL DROGO> , dies prompting her to halt the march and send three of her bloodriders in three different directions to scout for sustenance and refuge . 
the north remembers is the first episode of the second season of game of thrones . it is the eleventh episode of the series overall . it premiered on <APRIL> 1 , 2012. it was written by executive producers david benioff d.b . <WEISS> and directed by co executive producer alan taylor . 
under the burning <RED COMET> in the sky , war grips the continent of <WESTEROS> . in king's <LANDING> , <TYRION LANNISTER> arrives at court to serve as acting <HAND> of the king , and to rein in his crazed nephew king <JOFFREY BARATHEON> , as well as queen regent cersei . at <DRAGONSTONE> , <STANNIS BARATHEON> begins his quest to take the <IRON THRONE> with the help of a mysterious foreign priestess . on the eastern continent , <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> leads her people through the <RED WASTE> . <BEYOND> the wall , rangers , led by lord commander <JEOR MORMONT> , seek help from a dangerous wildling . 

in the <RIVERLANDS> , <ARYA STARK> continues to pose as a boy while traveling north with <YOREN> and his night's <CITY WATCH> recruits , and urinates privately . she is drawn to the caged prisoners jaqen <CITY WATCH>'ghar , rorge and <BITER> when jaqen asks her for water and introduces himself . a pair of gold cloaks approach the party and <ARYA STARK> hides , believing that they have come for her . they deliver a warrant for the royal bastard <GENDRY> but <YOREN> intimidates them into leaving empty handed . they promise to return with more <TOMMEN> . 
 <ARYA STARK> asks <GENDRY> why he is wanted and he admits that he does not know . he tells her that he was questioned by lord <JON ARRYN> and lord <EDDARD STARK> in the months before he fled king's <LANDING> . he questions why she thought that they had come for her and tells her that he has seen through her disguise . <ARYA STARK> reveals her identity to him and swears him to secrecy . 
in king's <LANDING> , <VARYS> discovers <SHAE> living with <TYRION LANNISTER> in the tower of the <HAND> and makes implied threats about revealing her presence . <TYRION LANNISTER> warns <VARYS> not to underestimate him . <ALTON LANNISTER> delivers king <ROBB STARK>'s peace terms to the <SMALL COUNCIL> and queen regent <CERSEI LANNISTER> rejects them . <GRAND> maester <PYCELLE> relays a message from the night's <CITY WATCH> requesting manpower and warning of wights . <TYRION LANNISTER> is the only one to take the warning seriously . 
ros struggles to continue her work as a prostitute having witnessed the murder of the infant royal bastard barra . <PETYR> baelish threatens her with a tale about selling an unhappy girl to a depraved customer in order to recoup his investment . he orders her to return happy after a night off . 
 <TYRION LANNISTER> has lord <JANOS SLYNT> for dinner and questions him about the massacre of the royal bastards . <JANOS SLYNT> freely admits his involvement but will not reveal who ordered the attack . <TYRION LANNISTER> has <JANOS SLYNT> arrested and exiled to the night's <CITY WATCH> and installs bronn as commander of the <CITY WATCH> in his place . <CERSEI LANNISTER> confronts <TYRION LANNISTER> about his actions . he warns that she is losing the support of the people but she claims that she does not care . he concludes that <JOFFREY BARATHEON> ordered the massacre , having initially suspected that it was <CERSEI LANNISTER> . he jokes about her relationship with <JAIME LANNISTER> and she says that he has always been funny . she ends the discussion with the barb that his finest joke was killing their mother when he was born . 
on <DRAGONSTONE> , <DAVOS> recruits the lysene sellsail <SALLADHOR> saan and his fleet of thirty ships to king <STANNIS BARATHEON>'s cause . his son <MATTHOS> seaworth encourages him to learn to read so that he can study the holy texts of the lord of <LIGHT> but <DAVOS> is happy to put his faith solely in <STANNIS BARATHEON> . <MELISANDRE> seduces <STANNIS BARATHEON> with the promise of a son . at first , <STANNIS BARATHEON> hesitates claiming he has a wife but <MELISANDRE> still manages to successfully seduce <STANNIS BARATHEON> .

what is dead may never die is the third episode of the second season of game of thrones . it is the thirteenth episode of the series overall . it premiered on <APRIL> 15 , 2012. it was written by story editor bryan cogman and directed by cinematographer alik sakharov . 
 <CATELYN STARK> treats with king <RENLY> in the hope of winning an alliance . <TYRION LANNISTER> undertakes a complex plan in king's <LANDING> to expose an enemy . at winterfell , <BRAN STARK>'s dreams continue to trouble him . 

a silent sister working on a casualty at <OXCROSS> . 
the <NORTHERN> <ARMY> under king <ROBB STARK> leads a surprise night time assault against an encamped <TYRION LANNISTER> <ARMY> , which was only manned by rennick and another <TYRION LANNISTER> guardsman garden of bones , with his direwolf <GREY WIND> causing a considerable amount of damage . the <BATTLE> of <OXCROSS> is a smashing victory , following through on <ROBB STARK>'s promise to give <CERSEI LANNISTER> another <WHISPERING WOOD> . 2 the next day <ROBB STARK> surveys the battlefield as <SILENT SISTERS> tend to both <ROBB STARK> and <CERSEI LANNISTER> wounded , while his bannerman , lord <ROOSE BOLTON> of the <DREADFORT> , argues that they should kill all of the <CERSEI LANNISTER> soldiers they took prisoner , because they're having trouble supplying their own <ARMY> and prisoners will slow them down . <ROBB STARK> disagrees , saying they will fight honorably and follow the laws of war . <ROOSE BOLTON> concedes that some of the <CERSEI LANNISTER> officers might have useful information they could be tortured into revealing , but <ROBB STARK> refuses , not wanting to give the <LANNISTERS> an excuse to torture his <SILENT SISTERS> , <SANSA STARK> and <ARYA STARK> . 
 <ROBB STARK> sees a woman battlefield healer treating a wounded <CERSEI LANNISTER> soldier . the prisoner protests when she tells him she has to amputate in order to save his life . <ROBB STARK> helps <HOLD> him down as she saws off the leg . the woman , who introduces herself as <TALISA> of <VOLANTIS> , criticizes <ROBB STARK> for the need for this war . <ROBB STARK> doesn't want the <IRON THRONE> , just revenge on joffrey for his father's death . she is shocked to learn he doesn't care which king takes the <IRON THRONE> after they defeat joffrey having declared for neither of the <STANNIS BARATHEON> <BROTHERS> . he just wants them to leave the north alone <AFTERWARD> . she points out that for all the bloodshed they have caused , he hasn't hurt the ones who killed his father , joffrey and <TYWIN LANNISTER> . the <TOMMEN> they slaughtered were not <TYWIN LANNISTER>'s main <ARMY> but unwilling boy soldiers and conscripts from the westerlands . 
the prisoners arrive at harrenhal . 
 <ARYA STARK> , <GENDRY> , and <HOT PIE> are taken by ser <AMORY LORCH>'s group of soldiers to harrenhal , a vast but partially ruined castle which was badly damaged during the targaryen conquest three hundred years ago by dragons' fire . <ARYA STARK>'s group is herded in with many other prisoners the <TYWIN LANNISTER> soldiers have taken , primarily peasant refugees from the <RIVERLANDS> . the commander of the entire <TYWIN LANNISTER> force is ser <GREGOR CLEGANE> , the mountain that rides , previously declared an outlaw by <EDDARD STARK> for his raiding in the <RIVERLANDS> . now the positions are reversed , with <GREGOR CLEGANE> having the support of the <IRON THRONE> to brutalize the rivermen . the stench of corpses is so strong that <ARYA STARK> notices it as soon as they are in <SIGHT> of the castle . the <TYWIN LANNISTER> soldiers under ser <GREGOR CLEGANE> particularly one known as the <TICKLER> sadistically torture many of the prisoners they have taken . one method used is to tie a bucket containing a rat to a woman's abdomen , and then to <HOLD> a flame to the back of the bucket so the rat will chew its way through the woman's guts . the prisoners are for the most part simple peasant refugees with no knowledge of the war , and the <TYWIN LANNISTER> soldiers are savagely torturing them just because they want to know where they may have hid the few valuables they have . however , some are also asked if they know anything about a group known as the brotherhood . just as <GENDRY> is about to be tortured , lord <TYWIN LANNISTER> arrives with the main host of his <ARMY> , who have retreated to harrenhal to regroup after their loss at the <BATTLE> of the <WHISPERING WOOD> . the <MAIN LANNISTER> <ARMY> group led by lord <TYWIN LANNISTER> is settling in to use harrenhal as their new <MAIN LANNISTER> base for the ongoing campaign in the <RIVERLANDS> . 
leave her face , i like her pretty . 
 <TYWIN LANNISTER> orders an immediate halt to the tortures saving <GENDRY> , rationally pointing out how disproportionate it is relative to what little wealth the peasants might be hiding , and it would be far more efficient to put them to work around the castle . as a blacksmith's apprentice , <GENDRY>'s skills are of particular use to them , and he is set to work . <TYWIN LANNISTER> instantly notices that arry is really a girl dressed up in boy's clothing , criticizing his soldiers for being too foolish to notice . when he asks her why she's dressed as a boy , <ARYA STARK> simply explains that it was safer . <TYWIN LANNISTER> is impressed with her intelligence , and takes her on as his new cupbearer while his <ARMY> is based at the castle . 
in king's <LANDING> , king <JOFFREY BARATHEON> is furious when he hears of <ROBB STARK>'s decisive victory against <TYWIN LANNISTER> forces . he has <SANSA STARK> brought before the assembled court in the recently redecorated <IRON THRONE> room , which now boasts <IRON THRONE> spikes on many surfaces and roaring fires surrounding the pillars . <LANCEL LANNISTER> tells <SANSA STARK> and the assembled nobles that <ROBB STARK> only won the <BATTLE> with trickery and sorcery . at first , <JOFFREY BARATHEON> sadistically menaces <SANSA STARK> by brandishing a crossbow at her and openly toying with the thought of killing her right in front of the <IRON THRONE> to send her brother a message . despite being clearly terrified , <SANSA STARK> refuses to give <JOFFREY BARATHEON> the satisfaction of scaring her and continues to firmly pledge her loyalty . annoyed , he reluctantly concedes to his mother's insistence that they need <SANSA STARK> alive , lowering the crossbow and ordering her to stand . . 
 <SANSA STARK> , beaten and stripped in front of the entire court . 
 <JOFFREY BARATHEON> then sits down on the <IRON THRONE> and commands ser <MERYN TRANT> of the <KINGSGUARD> to beat and strip her as punishment , but instructs <MERYN TRANT> to leave her face because i like her pretty . ser <MERYN TRANT> punches <SANSA STARK> violently in the stomach and strikes her in the back of the legs with the flat of his sword , causing her to fall down . he then rips open the back of her gown , leaving her partially naked from the waist up . as the beating continues , the entire court watches in horror , particularly a disgusted <SANDOR CLEGANE> . but despite being filled with dozens of knights and officials , no one intervenes out of fear of <JOFFREY BARATHEON>'s wrath . 
a furious <TYRION LANNISTER> marches in and puts a stop to the spectacle . he orders someone to cover <SANSA STARK> up and <SANDOR CLEGANE> immediately steps forward , taking off his cloak and proceeds to gently wrap it around her . <TYRION LANNISTER> turns his wrath upon <JOFFREY BARATHEON> , berating his actions as <SANSA STARK> is his future wife and queen that he is publicly shaming and the fact that <JOFFREY BARATHEON> doesn't pause to think how politically disastrous it would be for their allies to see him having his guards beat a valuable political hostage to a bloody pulp . furious , <JOFFREY BARATHEON> proclaims that he was punishing her . denouncing his nephew as a halfwit , <TYRION LANNISTER> points out the absurdity of punishing <SANSA STARK> for her brother's actions miles away in a war that <JOFFREY BARATHEON> himself started . now completely enraged , <JOFFREY BARATHEON> bellows that as king , he can do whatever he pleases , but <TYRION LANNISTER> again coldly counters that the <MAD> king thought he could do as he pleased too , which led to him being overthrown and killed . 
 <JOFFREY BARATHEON> torments ros to send a message to <TYRION LANNISTER> .

as <TYRION LANNISTER> works in his chamber late at knight , his cousin <LANCEL LANNISTER> knocks on his door delivering orders from <CERSEI LANNISTER> to release <GRAND> maester <PYCELLE> from the dungeon at once . despite their blood relationship <LANCEL LANNISTER> clearly holds <TYRION LANNISTER> in contempt and openly calls him <IMP> . curious , <TYRION LANNISTER> asks why <LANCEL LANNISTER> is so late delivering the message . blundering into a rather obvious trap , <LANCEL LANNISTER> retorts that he always delivers messages immediately and is never late . <TYRION LANNISTER> then simply points out how odd it is that <LANCEL LANNISTER> would be coming from <CERSEI LANNISTER>'s bedchambers in the middle of the knight . <LANCEL LANNISTER> nervously says <CERSEI LANNISTER> often works tirelessly keeping late hours , but <TYRION LANNISTER> also notices that he reeks of <CERSEI LANNISTER>'s favorite lavender oil perfume . <TYRION LANNISTER> enquires whether <LANCEL LANNISTER> was made a knight before or after he started sharing <CERSEI LANNISTER>'s bed . <LANCEL LANNISTER> falls apart , saying that <CERSEI LANNISTER>'s father ordered him to obey her every command when he became a squire to king <ROBERT BARATHEON> . <TYRION LANNISTER> sarcastically asks if <CERSEI LANNISTER> forced him to have sex with her too . <TYRION LANNISTER> wonders aloud what <JOFFREY BARATHEON> would do if he found out that <LANCEL LANNISTER> had not only killed <JOFFREY BARATHEON>'s father but was also sleeping with his mother . <LANCEL LANNISTER> gets down on his knees and pleads for his life . <TYRION LANNISTER> gently instructs <LANCEL LANNISTER> that he won't tell , but from now on , <LANCEL LANNISTER> must report everything <CERSEI LANNISTER> does back to <TYRION LANNISTER> . as <LANCEL LANNISTER> leaves , he also casually agrees that he will accede to <CERSEI LANNISTER>'s request and free <PYCELLE> if she wants him as a pet , though he doesn't want him back on the <SMALL COUNCIL> .

the main gate of <QARTH> opens for daenerys . 
on the return of her bloodrider kovarro , daenerys receives word that the city of <QARTH> is nearby , and they are willing to receive the mother of dragons . ser <JORAH MORMONT> cautions that the desert surrounding <QARTH> is known as the garden of bones , as those who are turned away by <QARTH> perish <OUTSIDE> the city walls due to exposure and thirst . daenerys and her khalasar leave the <RED WASTE> and reach the city of <QARTH> . the <THIRTEEN> , a group of wealthy nobles and merchant princes , the leaders of <QARTH> , emerge to greet her , guarded by a group of shielded spearmen . one of the <THIRTEEN> , the spice king , speaks for the group . they request that the mother of dragons present her children , but daenerys insists that her people be fed and sheltered before she reveals her dragons . the <THIRTEEN> decide to turn daenerys' group away and abandon them to the garden of bones . daenerys swears vengeance on <QARTH> , with fire and blood , should they not comply . <JORAH MORMONT> seems to find these threats rather reckless , but one of the <THIRTEEN> , <XARO> xhoan daxos , chooses to vouch for daenerys through sumai , a blood oath by which a qartheen may vouch for a visitor . daenerys and her khalasar are let into <QARTH> . 
the episode won a creative arts emmy award for art direction in a single camera series in september 2012 1 .
