a blind <ARYA STARK> resumes her training with the <WAIF> and jaqen <DOSH KHALEEN>'ghar , the former of whom beats her repeatedly when she lies . meanwhile , jaqen has her mixing potions blindly . during her training , <ARYA STARK> continues sparring with the <WAIF> while answering questions about her family and the <HOUND> . <ARYA STARK> admits to leaving the <HOUND> to die instead of killing him , despite wanting his death . the <WAIF> then interrogates <ARYA STARK> about the people on her list cersei , <GREGOR CLEGANE> and <WALDER FREY> . the <WAIF> voices her disbelief that <ARYA STARK>'s list is so short , but <ARYA STARK> counters by asking which name she wants added . when <ARYA STARK> insists that she is no one , the <WAIF> does not believe her and tries to hit her . however , <ARYA STARK> is able to deflect her blow and leap out of the way , surprising the <WAIF> . after confirming that <ARYA STARK> has mastered blind sparring , jaqen approaches <ARYA STARK> and offers to give back her <SIGHT> if she tells him her name . <ARYA STARK> replies that a girl has no name . jaqen then leads <ARYA STARK> to the well where he scoops up a bowl of water , which he offers her . she is reluctant , as others have drunk from it and died , but he says that if she is truly no one there is nothing to fear . <ARYA STARK> drinks from the bowl and her <SIGHT> is restored . when jaqen asks <ARYA STARK> who she is , she replies that she is no one . 
the umbers led by <SMALLJON> umber travel to winterfell to meet <RAMSAY BOLTON> , the new lord of winterfell and warden of the north . <SMALLJON> and <RAMSAY BOLTON> chat about their experiences with their fathers . <SMALLJON> mentions that his father <GREATJON> umber is dead but admits that he would have killed him if the opportunity arose . <RAMSAY BOLTON> denies murdering the late <ROOSE BOLTON> and claims that he was poisoned by his enemies , but <SMALLJON> doesn't bother believing him . 
 <SMALLJON> has come to forge an alliance with the <BOLTONS> against <JON SNOW> and the <WILDLINGS> . however , he refuses to bow to <RAMSAY BOLTON> citing the late <ROBB STARK>'s betrayal at the hands of <ROOSE BOLTON> . <SMALLJON> then reveals that he has a gift for <RAMSAY BOLTON> , who asks if it is a girl , hoping for <SANSA STARK> . <SMALLJON> replies otherwise and umber guards enter the room with two hooded figures . the first turns out to be <OSHA> the <SECOND SONS> is <RICKON> <SANSA STARK> , <NED STARK>'s youngest child . <OSHA> and <RICKON> appear uncomfortable to find themselves in <RAMSAY BOLTON>'s presence . when <RAMSAY BOLTON> asks <SMALLJON> to verify <RICKON>'s identity , an umber retainer enters the room carrying the severed head of the direwolf <SHAGGYDOG> , and <RICKON>'s expression of dismay confirms this was his pet . satisfied , a gleeful <RAMSAY BOLTON> then issues a sarcastic welcome <HOME> lord <NED STARK> . 
 <OATHBREAKER> is the third episode of the sixth season of game of thrones . it is the fifty third episode of the series overall . it premiered on may 8 , 2016. it was written by david benioff and d.b . <WEISS> , and directed by daniel sackheim . 
 <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> meets her future . bran meets the past . <TOMMEN> confronts the <HIGH SPARROW> . <ARYA STARK> trains to be no one . <VARYS> finds an answer . <RAMSAY BOLTON> gets a gift . 

underneath the great sept of baelor , <SEPTA UNELLA> enters queen <MARGAERY TYRELL>'s cell and leads her to a private meeting with the <HIGH SPARROW> . the <HIGH SPARROW> asks her what she would do if he allowed her to leave that day . <MARGAERY TYRELL> replied that she wants to return to her family and her husband <TOMMEN> baratheon . the <HIGH SPARROW> respects her love for her family but tells her that attachment leads to sin , citing his experience as a cobbler . <MARGAERY TYRELL> manages to impress the <HIGH SPARROW> with her knowledge of the book of the stranger , which she admits <SEPTA UNELLA> had read at her . the <HIGH SPARROW> chuckles and agrees that <SEPTA UNELLA> has a habit of reading at people instead of to them . 
the <HIGH SPARROW> recounts how in his youth he was a womanizer and drunkard . he underwent a conversion experience the morning after an orgy , as his drunken guests lay naked all around his house . tired of what he was now perceiving as a meaningless existence , the <HIGH SPARROW> then turned his life around and became a devoted member of the faith of the seven . he then left his job as a cobbler and devoted his life to the poor and destitute . believing he has found a way to reach <MARGAERY TYRELL> , the <HIGH SPARROW> allows her to visit her brother <LORAS> <MARGAERY TYRELL> . 
 <MARGAERY TYRELL> remaining in her cell . 
she finds a dejected <LORAS> lying on the floor of his cell . <LORAS> has lost the will to continue resisting but <MARGAERY TYRELL> tells him to stay strong because he is the future of <HOUSE TYRELL> . <LORAS> tells them that he only wants his imprisonment to end and pleads with her to help him . <MARGAERY TYRELL> tells <LORAS> that the <HIGH SPARROW> is trying to use them to break each other and again tells him to stay strong . 
at the <RED KEEP> , <CERSEI LANNISTER> walks in on <GRAND> maester <PYCELLE> advising king <TOMMEN> to accommodate the <HIGH SPARROW> and the <FAITH MILITANT> . <CERSEI LANNISTER> requests that <PYCELLE> leave the room while she talks to her son alone under the pretext of meeting him for updates about the previous <SMALL COUNCIL> meetings . during their conversation , <TOMMEN> proposes that the <IRON THRONE> not antagonize the <SPARROWS> further in order to avoid endangering <MARGAERY TYRELL>'s life . <CERSEI LANNISTER> then reminds her son about the humiliation that she endured at their hands and exploits <TOMMEN>'s love for <MARGAERY TYRELL> . she convinces her son that the <HIGH SPARROW> has no respect for kings , queens , and society . <TOMMEN> then reveals a secret that the <HIGH SPARROW> shared with him . 
armed with this new information , <CERSEI LANNISTER> barges into a <SMALL COUNCIL> meeting between <KEVAN> <CERSEI LANNISTER> , <OLENNA TYRELL> , and <JAIME LANNISTER> . while <KEVAN> and <OLENNA TYRELL> are initially hostile , <CERSEI LANNISTER> convinces them to listen to her . she then informs the <SMALL COUNCIL> that the <HIGH SPARROW> has planned to make <MARGAERY TYRELL> do the walk of atonement . <OLENNA TYRELL> is horrified that the <SPARROWS> plan to debase her granddaughter . <JAIME LANNISTER> then urges the <SMALL COUNCIL> to allow the <TYRELLS> to march their <ARMY> into king's <LANDING> , crush the <FAITH MILITANT> , and bring <MARGAERY TYRELL> and <LORAS> back to the <RED KEEP> into crown custody . <KEVAN> says that <TOMMEN> expressly forbid him to use the <JAIME LANNISTER> <ARMY> he commands at the city to make a move against the great sept , for fear that the <FAITH MILITANT> will harm <MARGAERY TYRELL> in retaliation . <JAIME LANNISTER> suggests that <OLENNA TYRELL> send <HOUSE TYRELL>'s <ARMY> to the city instead , and points out to his uncle that <TOMMEN> only forbade his <ARMY> from making a move but he never expressly told him to prevent anyone else from trying , so <KEVAN> wouldn't be breaking any commands if his forces simply stand down when the <HOUSE TYRELL> <ARMY> arrives . the <HOUSE TYRELL> <ARMY> will surround the great sept , intimidating the <SPARROWS> into releasing <MARGAERY TYRELL> and <LORAS> , without any blood actually being shed and by the time <TOMMEN> finds out what they've done he will already be happy with the outcome . <KEVAN>'s interest is now turned , but he still expresses reluctance should they fail . <CERSEI LANNISTER> is able to make him change his mind by exploiting his hatred towards the <SPARROWS> for taking his last remaining son and heir <LANCEL LANNISTER> . <OLENNA TYRELL> agrees that blood will be shed no matter what they do at this point , so it's better if it's the <SPARROWS>' blood and not theirs .

at <CASTLE BLACK> , <EDDISON> tollett helps <JON SNOW> pack up his things . edd scolds <JON SNOW> for leaving the night's watch after taking an oath , to which <JON SNOW> replies that he gave his life for the night's watch and can't trust his <BROTHERS> . at that moment , the horns sound for the arrival of travellers . <SANSA STARK> , <BRIENNE> of tarth and <PODRICK> payne ride through the gates and dismount in the courtyard . <JON SNOW> rushes out and sees <SANSA STARK> for the first time since the <STARKS> left winterfell for king's <LANDING> , and they embrace . later that night , they converse and reminisce on their childhood . <SANSA STARK> proposes they take winterfell back from <RAMSAY BOLTON> but <JON SNOW> says he's done fighting , especially after hanging <OLLY> . 
 <JON SNOW> and <SANSA STARK> are reunited at the wall . 
 <DAVOS> seaworth asks whether <MELISANDRE> will stay at <CASTLE BLACK> and she replies she will do as <JON SNOW> , the prince that was promised , commands . <DAVOS> asks what happened to stannis and she replies he was defeated in <BATTLE> . when he asks about <SHIREEN> , <MELISANDRE> is reluctant to speak . their conversation is interrupted by <BRIENNE> , who recognizes <DAVOS> and <MELISANDRE> as stannis' former entourage . still bitter over the death of king <RENLY> baratheon , <BRIENNE> warns <MELISANDRE> that she does not forget or forgive . she also tells them that she executed stannis after he admitted using blood magic to assassinate <RENLY> . 
some time later , <JON SNOW> receives a letter from <RAMSAY BOLTON> stating that he has <RICKON> <SANSA STARK> at winterfell and if <SANSA STARK> is not returned , he will slaughter every wildling at <CASTLE BLACK> , let his <TOMMEN> rape <SANSA STARK> , and feed <JON SNOW> and <RICKON> to his dogs . <TORMUND> says he has 2 , 000 able fighters , far less than the estimated 5 , 000 <RAMSAY BOLTON> has . <SANSA STARK> says that they have to try to retake their <HOME> and rescue their brother and that the houses of the north will unite behind <JON SNOW> as the son of the true warden of the north . <JON SNOW> resolves to take <RAMSAY BOLTON> down .

 <ROBIN> practices his archery . 
at runestone , <ROBIN> arryn trains at his archery in front of lord yohn <ROYCE> . <PETYR> baelish arrives with a retinue of arryn guards and a pet falcon as a belated name day gift . <ROYCE> reminds baelish that he told him that he was taking <SANSA STARK> with him to the <FINGERS> , but he received word that she had been married to <RAMSAY BOLTON> . baelish tells him that on the way to the <FINGERS> they were set upon by a large force of <RAMSAY BOLTON> <TOMMEN> . a confrontation ensues , in which <PETYR> accuses <ROYCE> of giving away the information regarding the location of <SANSA STARK> to <HOUSE BOLTON> . when <ROYCE> accuses baelish of slander , <PETYR> reminds him that <ROBIN> is the lord of the <VALE> , and asks for his judgment . <ROBIN> then asks baelish if they should throw lord <ROYCE> from the <MOON DOOR> , which prompts the surrounding knights , including those loyal to <ROYCE> , to muster themselves . <ROYCE> swears his loyalty to <ROBIN> , and he is let off without punishment on baelish's recommendation . <ROYCE> comes onto the dark realization that <LITTLEFINGER> has control over <ROBIN> . <PETYR> and <ROBIN> decide they have to muster the <VALE> knights to march north and aid <SANSA STARK> . 
at winterfell , <OSHA> is brought before <RAMSAY BOLTON> , who says that while her fellow captive <RICKON> <SANSA STARK> has value to <RAMSAY BOLTON> , he is unsure of her worth . <OSHA> denounces the <STARKS> , saying that her servitude and loyalty to them were forced . she also attempts to seduce <RAMSAY BOLTON> , climbing onto his lap and kissing him , all the while trying to get the knife he had been using to peel apples . <RAMSAY BOLTON> seemingly falls for it , saying that it took much longer for him to get <THEON GREYJOY> over to his side but that <THEON GREYJOY> told him everything , including how <OSHA> had seduced <THEON GREYJOY> in order to help <RICKON> and <BRAN STARK> escape winterfell . <OSHA> realizes that she has been lured into a trap , and tries to stab <RAMSAY BOLTON> , only for him to slash her throat . she dies shortly thereafter .

 <THEON GREYJOY> returns <HOME> . 
 <THEON GREYJOY> returns <HOME> to <PYKE> , where he learns of the death of his father , <BALON GREYJOY> . his sister , <YARA> , is unhappy about his return and his refusal to leave the <DREADFORT> when she made an attempt to rescue <THEON GREYJOY> from <RAMSAY BOLTON> . <THEON GREYJOY> explains that <RAMSAY BOLTON> broke him into a thousand pieces , which <YARA> affirms yes , he sent us one of those pieces referring to the box containing <THEON GREYJOY>'s penis that she and <BALON GREYJOY> received . <YARA> then suspects that <THEON GREYJOY> has come back to declare himself king of the <IRON ISLANDS> , but he insists that he does not want the crown , instead wishing for <YARA> to rule , with him helping her in any way that he can .

 <TYRION LANNISTER> along with <GREY WORM> , <MISSANDEI> , and <VARYS> meet with representatives of the good masters of <ASTAPOR> , the <WISE MASTERS> of yunkai , and the slave trading city of <VOLANTIS> who have arrived by sea . as the diplomatic mission enters the harbor , <GREY WORM> advocates using military force . when <TYRION LANNISTER> explains that he is able to empathize with slaves because he spent one day as a slave , <MISSANDEI> counters that he has not experienced slavery . the emissaries are <TYRION LANNISTER>'s former slave master <YEZZAN> zo qaggaz , the yunkai'i <WISE MASTERS> master <RAZDAL> mo eraz and the volantene triarch belicho paenymion . 
 <VARYS> , <TYRION LANNISTER> and <MISSANDEI> converge to prepare for their meeting . 
in their meeting chambers , <YEZZAN> marvels at how <TYRION LANNISTER> went from being a nearly worthless slave to the de facto ruler of <MEEREEN> . the slave trading cities offer to give <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> and her mercenaries a large pot of money if they sail away from <SLAVER>'s <BAY> . when <MISSANDEI> defends <DAENERYS TARGARYEN>'s actions in liberating slaves , <RAZDAL> contends that slavery has existed for centuries . after hearing their offer , <TYRION LANNISTER> proposes a counter offer . he offers to give them a seven year grace period to phase out slavery and to compensate slave owners , however they must end all backing for the sons of the harpy regardless of whether they admit this backing or not . he then cautions them that they will not get a better offer . <TYRION LANNISTER> then gives them time to consider his offer , though <GREY WORM> and <MISSANDEI> insist on abolishing slavery . 
 <TYRION LANNISTER> and his entourage are later confronted by a crowd of former slaves in the <MEEREEN> throne room . a freedman demands to know when <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> will return while another is appalled at the idea of <TYRION LANNISTER> negotiating with slave traders . <TYRION LANNISTER> insists he is doing his best to rule the city in <DAENERYS TARGARYEN>'s absence . the freedmen do not trust <TYRION LANNISTER> , a foreigner and a newcomer , and look to <GREY WORM> and <MISSANDEI> for reassurance . despite their misgivings , they both publicly back <TYRION LANNISTER>'s diplomacy in front of the freedmen . in private , <GREY WORM> and <MISSANDEI> warn <TYRION LANNISTER> that the <WISE MASTERS> will outmaneuver him , despite his best efforts to do the same to them .

ser <JORAH MORMONT> and <DAARIO> <NAHARIS> approach the outskirts of <VAES DOTHRAK> and discard their weapons , as drawing a blade in the city is considered sacrilege . within the city itself , <JORAH MORMONT> and <DAARIO> run afoul of <AKHO> and <IGGO> who see through <JORAH MORMONT>'s claims to be a wine merchant . <DAARIO> takes care of <IGGO> while <AKHO> tackles <JORAH MORMONT> . the knight is nearly undone , but <DAARIO> saves him at the last minute with the stiletto he smuggled in . at <JORAH MORMONT>'s insistence , <DAARIO> smashes aggo's skull with a rock so that no one will think he was killed with a bladed weapon . 
 <DANY> proves to the dothraki who their true khaleesi is . 
meanwhile , the high priestess of the <DOSH KHALEEN> gives <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> a commentary on the other crones . some of them hate <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> , thinking the dothraki should not interbreed with other races , but the high priestess dismisses them , saying that the dothraki have always interbred and have never been concerned with blood purity . to illustrate her point , the high priestess indicates another of the <DOSH KHALEEN> , a <LHAZAREEN> girl <ORNELA> taken from her village at the age of twelve . <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> asks to relieve herself , and the high priestess sends <ORNELA> with her . as they walk , <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> learns that <ORNELA>'s khal died when she was only sixteen . the pair are interrupted by <JORAH MORMONT> and <DAARIO> , who take the <LHAZAREEN> hostage . <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> , unsurprised to see them , cancels their plans for escape they have a slim chance of leaving <VAES DOTHRAK> , let alone getting back to <MEEREEN> and tells them that she has a plan of her own . she asks <ORNELA> if she is willing to help them , calling her a khaleesi queen instead of a <DOSH KHALEEN> crone . the girl reluctantly agrees . 
during the khalar vezhven , the khals argue about how to deal with <IGGO> and <AKHO>'s deaths <KHAL MORO> defuses the situation by reminding them that ahko was a member of his khalasar , and he does not care about finding the killer if he was stupid enough to get himself killed . <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> is then brought in by the two priestesses she befriended before . <KHAL MORO> insists that she join the <DOSH KHALEEN> , but another <KHAL MORO> expresses interest in making her his khaleesi , while another suggests giving her to the <WISE MASTERS> in exchange for ten thousand horses . <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> dismisses all of them she claims that they are all petty and weak , and reminds them that <KHAL DROGO> was willing to cross the poison water in wooden horses for his conquests . 
 <JORAH MORMONT> and <DAARIO> bow down to their queen . 
stating that none of the khals is fit to lead the dothraki , <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> declares that she will lead them herself . after a pause , <KHAL MORO> and the khals burst into laughter . <DANY> reminds them that her husband , in the same temple in which they all now sit , declared that he would lead a dothraki <ARMY> across the <NARROW SEA> to retake the <IRON THRONE> for his khaleesi and that all the khals have done since is to raid and plunder villages in lieu of any meaningful conquest . disgusted with her insolence , <KHAL MORO> declares that she will be raped by each of the khals , then by all of their bloodriders , and then , if she is still alive , by their horses . <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> is unfazed by the threats , as she knocks down the braziers in the hut , setting everything aflame . the khals desperately attempt to escape the rapidly spreading fire , only to find the temple's only door barred , the bodies of the two men guarding it lying dead <OUTSIDE> . 
as the flames climb higher , the <DOSH KHALEEN> and khalasars gather in confusion . eventually , the doors collapse and <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> emerges , naked and unburned , with the entire leadership present at <VAES DOTHRAK> dead . many of the assembled bow immediately , with the high priestess and the rest of the <DOSH KHALEEN> following after a moment . <JORAH MORMONT> and <DAARIO> move to the front of the crowd and bow last . 
book of the stranger is the fourth episode of the sixth season of game of thrones . it is the fifty fourth episode of the series overall . it premiered on may 15 , 2016. it was written by david benioff and d.b . <WEISS> , and directed by daniel sackheim . 
 <TYRION LANNISTER> strikes a deal . <JORAH MORMONT> and <DAARIO> undertake a difficult task . jaime and cersei try to improve their situation . jon and sansa reunite . 

sansa refuses <LITTLEFINGER>'s offer . 
 <SANSA STARK> receives a message bearing the sigil of <HOUSE BAELISH> , asking her to a meeting in <MOLE>'s <TOWN> . accompanied by <BRIENNE> , <SANSA STARK> furiously confronts <PETYR> <HOUSE BAELISH> , asking if he was aware what <RAMSAY BOLTON> was capable of . <HOUSE BAELISH> deflects , saying he has the knights of the <VALE> waiting at <MOAT CAILIN> to aid <SANSA STARK> . she is mistrustful of him when he claims he had no idea of <RAMSAY BOLTON>'s abusive treatment of her . she doubts <HOUSE BAELISH>'s ability to protect her or even himself , threatening to have <BRIENNE> kill him . he says he'll do whatever she asks and <SANSA STARK> tells him to leave and never come back for her . he obeys , but not before informing that her great uncle <BRYNDEN> tully has recaptured <RIVERRUN> and recommending she seek him out and the remaining loyal tully forces . <SANSA STARK> says she already has an <ARMY> , her brother <JON SNOW>'s <ARMY> of <WILDLINGS> . half brother , <HOUSE BAELISH> clarifies as he walks away , reminding her that <JON SNOW> is only her half brother . 
at <CASTLE BLACK> , a war council is called , and is attended by <SANSA STARK> , <BRIENNE> , <PODRICK> , <JON SNOW> , <DAVOS> , <MELISANDRE> , <TORMUND> and <EDDISON> tollett , who discuss the need for more men to defend <CASTLE BLACK> , since the <KARSTARKS> and umbers , two major houses in the north , have declared for <RAMSAY BOLTON> . <JON SNOW> points out that they can summon the rest of the minor houses , such as the mormonts , glovers , cerwyns , and mazins , to rival their enemies , and <SANSA STARK> reveals <BRYNDEN>'s successful retaking of <RIVERRUN> , though she claims she learned via one of <RAMSAY BOLTON>'s ravens in order to stop <JON SNOW> from pursuing <LITTLEFINGER> . <SANSA STARK> subsequently tasks <BRIENNE> and <PODRICK> with securing <BRYNDEN>'s help while the rest of them leave <CASTLE BLACK> to start building their <ARMY> . before leaving <CASTLE BLACK> , <SANSA STARK> presents <JON SNOW> with a new cloak like their father's , carrying the <SANSA STARK> sigil .

the <WAIF> continues to drill arya , mocking her high born origins . jaqen h ghar explains that the <FACELESS MEN> were slaves in <VALYRIA> before establishing the free city of <BRAAVOS> and the <HOUSE BAELISH> of <CASTLE BLACK> white . handing arya a vial , jaqen tells her an actress , lady <CRANE> , will be the next to receive the many faced god s gift . . 
arya watches the bloody <HAND> , a stage play in <BRAAVOS> loosely based on the recent civil wars in <WESTEROS> . 
arya enjoys the spectacle of the actors re enacting the war of the <FIVE KINGS> , playing <BARATHEONS> and <LANNISTERS> , but her pleasure ceases when her father , and his execution , are inaccurately caricatured . eddard is portrayed as a buffoon , and the actress who plays <SANSA STARK> has her breasts bared to the audience . arya sneaks into the dressing room after the play to observe her target the actress playing cersei who appears to be a clever , decent woman . arya later shares with jaqen her plan to poison lady <CRANE> s rum , which no one else in the troupe drinks . arya suspects that a jealous younger actress , bianca , has commissioned the kill . jaqen cuts her off , reminding her a servant does not question . 
 <JORAH MORMONT> shows his arm to <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> . 
 <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> is unsure of what to do with <JORAH MORMONT> , having banished him twice , seeing him defiantly return twice , and him twice saving her life . <JORAH MORMONT> finally confesses his love for <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> , but also reveals his spreading greyscale infection , and says that this time , he needs to leave for good . he starts to leave and states his plan to take his own life well before the greyscale envelops him , but <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> tearfully commands him to find a cure and come back to her side when she conquers <WESTEROS> . <JORAH MORMONT> then departs while <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> and <DAARIO> <NAHARIS> lead the dothraki horde back to <MEEREEN> .

 <KINVARA> , the high <RED PRIESTESS> . 
while the rulers of <MEEREEN> enjoy a tenuous peace , <TYRION LANNISTER> reminds them of the need to convince the meereenese that everything has been done with <DAENERYS TARGARYEN>'s blessing , as the <WISE MASTERS> could use <TYRION LANNISTER> and <VARYS>'s foreign status against them to reclaim <SLAVER>'s <BAY> . to that end , <TYRION LANNISTER> invites <KINVARA> , high <RED PRIESTESS> of the <RED PRIESTESS> temple of <VOLANTIS> , to negotiate spreading the word of <DAENERYS TARGARYEN>'s accomplishments . to <TYRION LANNISTER>'s surprise , <KINVARA> appears to be highly accommodating in supporting <TYRION LANNISTER>'s goals , as she firmly believes that <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> is the prince that was promised . <VARYS> is more skeptical , being suspicious of any practitioners of magic , and points out that <MELISANDRE> had already declared <STANNIS BARATHEON> to be the prince , only for him to be defeated twice . <KINVARA> says that while the lord of <LIGHT> has a plan , the humans following him do occasionally make errors . she then unnerves <VARYS> by revealing that she knows <VARYS> was emasculated by a second rate sorcerer and offers to repeat the words he heard in the flames , and identify who it was that spoke . <VARYS> is uncharacteristically unsettled by this revelation . <KINVARA> then assures <TYRION LANNISTER> that she will send the preachers and priests best suited to the task at <HAND> .

as the kingsmoot is held , <YARA> greyjoy is the first to lay claim to the <SALT THRONE> . <YARA> argues that raiding the mainland is not enough for their people , and that they need to use military force to teach the mainlanders a lesson . an <IRONBORN> woman challenges <YARA>'s candidacy on the grounds that she is a woman and points out that her brother <THEON GREYJOY> has returned . <THEON GREYJOY> endorses his older sister and urges the gathering to do the same stressing that she is a warrior , a reaver , and an <IRONBORN> . many shout for <YARA> to be their queen . 
before they can crown <YARA> , <EURON GREYJOY> joins the gathering to lay claim to the <SALT THRONE> . he openly mocks <THEON GREYJOY> for his military failures and emasculation before deriding <YARA> as a woman . <YARA> in turn accuses <EURON GREYJOY> of killing their king and her father balon . to her surprise , <EURON GREYJOY> admits killing balon but then defends his actions on the grounds that balon was leading them to defeat in the north . when <EURON GREYJOY> states that his only regret is not killing balon years earlier , he is met by resounding cheers from the crowd . <THEON GREYJOY> then counters that <EURON GREYJOY> had spent years gallivanting overseas while <YARA> was commanding <IRONBORN> ships and <FACELESS MEN> . <YARA> then suggests building a massive fleet to attack and make their mark on <WESTEROS> . 
 <EURON GREYJOY> , king of the <IRON ISLANDS> . 
in response , <EURON GREYJOY> announces that he also supports expanding the <IRONBORN> fleet . revealing a trick up his sleeve , he then proposes to marry <DAENERYS TARGARYEN> and then carry her <ARMY> and dragons back to <WESTEROS> . the <IRONBORN> support <EURON GREYJOY>'s plan and declare him king . the drowned <FACELESS MEN> priest <AERON> <EURON GREYJOY> then leads <EURON GREYJOY> down to the sea to be drowned and reborn , as is the custom . knowing that <EURON GREYJOY> will kill them as soon as he is able , <YARA> , <THEON GREYJOY> , and many of their loyalists flee the <IRON ISLANDS> during <EURON GREYJOY>'s coronation , taking much of the <IRON ISLANDS> fleet with them . after <EURON GREYJOY> revives himself , he is crowned by his brother <AERON> . after learning that his niece and nephew have fled with their best ships , <EURON GREYJOY> calls on his followers to build their own ships so that he may pursue the pair and kill them . 
b . 
the three eyed raven shows bran a vision of a heart tree amid spirals of standing stones in a lush green valley . his vision shows <LEAF> and other children of the <FOREST> talking amongst themselves , then looking eagerly at a captive bound to the tree . <LEAF> approaches and forces a dragonglass dagger into the captive's chest . the captive screams , but does not die , instead becoming the first white walker . 
bran immediately confronts <LEAF> about creating the <WHITE WALKERS> in the first place . <LEAF> tries to explain that they were at war with the <FIRST MEN> and were desperate . later , bran is the only one in the cave awake and is anxious to warg back into the <WEIRWOOD> tree . bran wargs into the tree by himself and sees the <ARMY> of the dead . he slowly walks through the <ARMY> until he comes to a space occupied by four <WHITE WALKERS> , including the night king . as bran becomes aware that the the night king and the dead are now able to see him , the night king grabs his arm , branding him with an icy mark . he breaks out of the vision with a scream waking the others . the three eyed raven tells bran , <MEERA> and <HODOR> that the night king is now able to locate bran and able to bypass the powerful magic keeping the <WHITE WALKERS> and the wights out of the cave . as a result , they must leave now and bran must become the three eyed raven . bran asks whether he is ready , and the raven says no at which point bran's eyes whiten as he enters another vision . 
as <MEERA> and <HODOR> are preparing to leave they notice the air is so cold their breath is visible , indicating the arrival of the <ARMY> of the dead <OUTSIDE> of the cave . the night king and three <WHITE WALKERS> start marching towards the cave . the children of the <FOREST> try using magic projectiles to fend the <WHITE WALKERS> off , but are overwhelmed . they <LIGHT> a fire around the entrance which prevents the wights from entering but the <WHITE WALKERS> extinguish a pathway and walk through . the wights end up climbing over the <WEIRWOOD> and dropping through roots at the top of the cave . <MEERA> desperately tries to get bran out of the vision and attempts to get the frightened <HODOR> to carry bran away to no avail . using a dragonglass tipped spear , <MEERA> kills the <FIRST MEN> <WHITE WALKERS> walker that enters , and fights alongside the remaining children of the <FOREST> to try to fend off the wights until bran wakes up . wights begin to swarm the cave , killing all of the children of the <FOREST> except for <LEAF> , as <MEERA> starts yelling at bran to warg into <HODOR> . 
in the vision , bran is at winterfell watching <NED STARK> say goodbye to his father , rickard <NED STARK> , before being sent to the <VALE> as a ward . while still in the vision , bran hears <MEERA>'s cries to warg into <HODOR> and the three eyed raven tells him to listen to her . bran wargs into both the present day <HODOR> in the cave and <WYLIS> , the young version of <HODOR> in his vision . 
 <WYLIS> seizing , as his words <HOLD> the door evolve into <HODOR> . 
the <HODOR> in the cave puts bran's body on a sled and starts hauling him down a tunnel leading out of the cave with <LEAF> and <MEERA> , as bran's direwolf <SUMMER> is killed attacking the wights . as the wights are closing in on them , <LEAF> sacrifices herself , using magic to cause a huge explosion , buying the other three enough time to get to a door at the end of the tunnel . while the three eyed raven and bran are still sharing a vision , the night king kills the three eyed raven , and his figure within bran's vision blows away as ashes and rags . 
with some difficulty <HODOR> pushes the door open and pulls bran through , coming back to help <MEERA> close the door just as the wights approach . <MEERA> grabs bran's sled and tells <HODOR> to bar the exit , shouting to <HOLD> the door . inside bran's vision , <WYLIS> notices bran , who links the present <HODOR> to the past <WYLIS> . <WYLIS> begins to seize when he enters the mind of his future self . as <MEERA> continues to yell <HOLD> the door to present day <HODOR> , within bran's vision <WYLIS> falls to the ground convulsing and starts repeating this same sentence in the midst of his seizure . eventually , <HOLD> the door slurs into <HODOR> , as his condition deteriorates and it becomes apparent this is the moment <HODOR> lost the ability to say any other words , and his destiny was fixed . 
present day <HODOR> braces himself against the door long enough for <MEERA> to disappear into the snow with bran's unconscious body on the sled . inevitably , the wights break through parts of the <WEIRWOOD> and begin scratching and stabbing a visibly distressed <HODOR> . with no possibility of escape , all that is shown at the end is young <WYLIS> in the past seizing and crying out <HODOR> . 
the door is the fifth episode of the sixth season of game of thrones . it is the fifty fifth episode of the series overall . it premiered on may 22 , 2016. it was written by david benioff and d.b . <WEISS> , and directed by jack bender . 
tyrion seeks a strange ally . bran learns a great deal . <BRIENNE> goes on a mission . arya is given a chance to prove herself .
